```python
import paho.mqtt.client as mqtt
import json

class AcrelMQTTListener:
    def __init__(self, broker_host, username, password):
        self.client = mqtt.Client()
        self.client.username_pw_set(username, password)
        self.client.on_connect = self.on_connect
        self.client.on_message = self.on_message
        self.client.connect(broker_host, 1883, 60)
    
    def on_connect(self, client, userdata, flags, rc):
        if rc == 0:
            # ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู ูู ููุงุถูุน ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
            client.subscribe("acrel/+/+/data")
            client.subscribe("acrel/+/+/status")
    
    def on_message(self, client, userdata, msg):
        payload = json.loads(msg.payload.decode())
        # ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
        self.process_meter_data(msg.topic, payload)
    
    def start(self):
        self.client.loop_forever()
```

#### ุงููููุฉ 3.3 (ูุญุณููุฉ): ุชุทููุฑ ูุงุดุฑ ุฃูุงูุฑ MQTT

|---|--------|-------|---------|------|
| 3.3.1 | ุจูุงุก AcrelService Class | ุฎุฏูุฉ ูุฑูุฒูุฉ | ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู | ููู |
| 3.3.2 | ูุธููุฉ disconnect() | ูุตู ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ | ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู | ููู |
| 3.3.3 | ูุธููุฉ reconnect() | ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ | ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู | ููู |
| 3.3.4 | ูุธููุฉ setTariff() | ุชุบููุฑ ุงูุชุนุฑูุฉ | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |
| 3.3.5 | ูุธููุฉ getReading() | ูุฑุงุกุฉ ููุฑูุฉ | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |
| 3.3.6 | ูุธุงู ุชุฃููุฏ ุงูุฃูุงูุฑ | Command Acknowledgment | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |
| 3.3.7 | ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุฃุฎุทุงุก | Error Handling | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
class AcrelService:
    def __init__(self, mqtt_client):
        self.client = mqtt_client
    
    def disconnect(self, meter_id, station_id, reason):
        """ูุตู ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ ุนู ุนุฏุงุฏ"""
        topic = f"acrel/{station_id}/{meter_id}/command"
        payload = {
            "command": "relay_off",
            "reason": reason,
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        self.client.publish(topic, json.dumps(payload))
    
    def reconnect(self, meter_id, station_id):
        """ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุชูุตูู ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ"""
        topic = f"acrel/{station_id}/{meter_id}/command"
        payload = {
            "command": "relay_on",
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        self.client.publish(topic, json.dumps(payload))
    
    def set_tariff(self, meter_id, station_id, tariff_id, effective_date):
        """ุชุบููุฑ ุงูุชุนุฑูุฉ"""
        topic = f"acrel/{station_id}/{meter_id}/command"
        payload = {
            "command": "set_tariff",
            "tariff_id": tariff_id,
            "effective_date": effective_date
        }
        self.client.publish(topic, json.dumps(payload))
```

#### ุงููููุฉ 3.4 (ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ): ุชุทููุฑ ูุญุฏุฉ ุชุญููู ุฌูุฏุฉ ุงูุทุงูุฉ

**ุงููุตู:** ุงุณุชุบูุงู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุบููุฉ ูู ุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ADW300.

| # | ุงููููุฉ | ุงููุตู | ุงูุฃููููุฉ | ุงููุฏุฉ |

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
class AcrelClient:
    def __init__(self, api_url, username, password):
        self.api_url = api_url
        self.session = self._authenticate(username, password)
    
    def get_device(self, device_id):
        """ุฌูุจ ุจูุงูุงุช ุฌูุงุฒ"""
        response = self.session.get(f"{self.api_url}/devices/{device_id}")
        return response.json()
    
    def get_meter_reading(self, meter_id):
        """ุฌูุจ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ุนุฏุงุฏ"""
        response = self.session.get(f"{self.api_url}/meters/{meter_id}/reading")
        return response.json()
    
    def control_relay(self, device_id, action):
        """ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงููุฑุญู"""
        payload = {"action": action}
        response = self.session.post(
            f"{self.api_url}/devices/{device_id}/relay",
            json=payload
        )
        return response.json()
    
    def get_historical_data(self, meter_id, start_date, end_date):
        """ุฌูุจ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุชุงุฑูุฎูุฉ"""
        params = {
            "start": start_date,
            "end": end_date
        }
        response = self.session.get(
            f"{self.api_url}/meters/{meter_id}/history",
            params=params
        )
        return response.json()
```

#### ุงููููุฉ 3: ุจูุงุก Webhook Endpoint (ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ)

| # | ุงููููุฉ | ุงููุตู | ุงูุฃููููุฉ | ุงููุฏุฉ |
|---|--------|-------|---------|------|
| 3.1 | ุจูุงุก Webhook Endpoint | ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช | ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู | ููู |
| 3.2 | ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุชูููุน | Signature Verification | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |
| 3.3 | ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุฅูุฐุงุฑุงุช | Process Alarms | ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู | ูููุงู |
| 3.4 | ุชูุฌูู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช | Route Notifications | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |
| 3.5 | ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฃุญุฏุงุซ | Event Logging | ุนุงููุฉ | ููู |

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
from flask import Flask, request

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route('/webhooks/acrel/alarm', methods=['POST'])
def handle_alarm():
    """ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช ุงูุฅูุฐุงุฑุงุช ูู Acrel"""
    
    # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุชูููุน
    signature = request.headers.get('X-Signature')
    if not verify_signature(request.data, signature):
        return {'error': 'Invalid signature'}, 401
    
    # ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุฅูุฐุงุฑ
    alarm_data = request.json
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุญุฏุซ
    log_event('alarm_received', alarm_data)
    
    # ุชูุฌูู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑ
    if alarm_data['severity'] == 'critical':
        send_sms_to_engineers(alarm_data)
    
    return {'status': 'received'}, 200
```

#### ุงููููุฉ 4: ุฑุจุท ุงูููุชุฑุฉ ุจุงูุชุญูู (ูุญุฏุซุฉ)

| # | ุงููููุฉ | ุงููุตู | ุงูุฃููููุฉ | ุงููุฏุฉ |
|---|--------|-------|---------|------|

**ููุทู ุงููุตู ูุงููุตู:**
```python
def check_and_disconnect_overdue_customers():
    """ูุญุต ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ุงููุชุฃุฎุฑุฉ ููุตู ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ"""
    
    overdue_invoices = Invoice.query.filter(
        Invoice.status == 'overdue',
        Invoice.days_overdue >= 7
    ).all()
    
    for invoice in overdue_invoices:
        meter = invoice.subscriber.meter
        
        # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงููุตู ุนุจุฑ API
        acrel_client.control_relay(
            device_id=meter.acrel_device_id,
            action='disconnect'
        )
        
        # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฃูุฑ
        log_command(
            meter_id=meter.id,
            action='disconnect',
            reason='overdue_payment'
        )

def check_and_reconnect_paid_customers():
    """ูุญุต ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ุงููุฏููุนุฉ ูุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ"""
    
    disconnected_meters = Meter.query.filter(
        Meter.status == 'disconnected'
    ).all()
    
    for meter in disconnected_meters:
        # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุณุฏุงุฏ ุฌููุน ุงูููุงุชูุฑ
        unpaid_invoices = Invoice.query.filter(
            Invoice.meter_id == meter.id,
            Invoice.status == 'unpaid'
        ).count()
        
        if unpaid_invoices == 0:
            # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงููุตู
            acrel_client.control_relay(
                device_id=meter.acrel_device_id,
                action='reconnect'
            )
            
            # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฃูุฑ
            log_command(
                meter_id=meter.id,
                action='reconnect',
                reason='payment_received'
            )
```

  - ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงููุฆุฉ ุงููุฎุชุงุฑุฉ

```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
class SubscriberSubsidy(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    subscriber_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('subscriber.id'))
    is_subsidized = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=False)
    subsidy_program_id = db.Column(db.Integer)
    subsidy_category = db.Column(db.String(10))  # 'A' or 'B'
    subsidy_reference_number = db.Column(db.String(50))
    subsidy_start_date = db.Column(db.Date)
    subsidy_end_date = db.Column(db.Date)
    monthly_quota_kwh = db.Column(db.Float)  # 82 or 64
    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)

# API ูุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุฏุนู
@app.route('/api/subscribers/<id>/subsidy', methods=['PUT'])
def update_subscriber_subsidy(id):
    subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(id)
    data = request.json
    
    subsidy = SubscriberSubsidy.query.filter_by(
        subscriber_id=id
    ).first_or_create()
    
    subsidy.is_subsidized = data.get('is_subsidized')
    subsidy.subsidy_category = data.get('category')
    subsidy.subsidy_reference_number = data.get('reference_number')
    subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh = 82 if data.get('category') == 'A' else 64
    
    db.session.commit()
    return {'status': 'success'}, 200
```

### 6.2: ุจูุงุก ูุญุฏุฉ ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุญุตุต ุงูุงุณุชููุงู (Quota Control Module)

**ุงููุตู:** ูููุฉ ูุฌุฏููุฉ ุชุนูู ูู ุจุฏุงูุฉ ูู ุดูุฑ ูุดุญู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุจุงูุญุตุฉ ุงููุฏุนููุฉ.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 6.2.1: ุจุฑูุฌุฉ Scheduled Job
  - ูุนูู ููููุงู ูู ุงูุณุงุนุฉ 12:01 ุตุจุงุญุงู (ุฃูู ููู ูู ุงูุดูุฑ)
  - ูุจุญุซ ุนู ุฌููุน ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู
  - ูุฑุณู ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงูุดุญู ุฅูู Acrel

- 6.2.2: ููุทู ุงูุดุญู ุงูุดูุฑู
  - ูุฑุงุกุฉ ุงูุญุตุฉ ุงููุฏุนููุฉ (82 ุฃู 64)
  - ุงุณุชุฏุนุงุก API Acrel ูุดุญู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ
  - ุชุณุฌูู ุนูููุฉ ุงูุดุญู ูู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช

- 6.2.3: ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุฃุฎุทุงุก ูุงูุงุณุชุซูุงุกุงุช
  - ุฅุฐุง ูุดู ุงูุดุญู: ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุงููุญุงููุฉ
  - ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ูุนุทูุงู: ุชุณุฌูู ุชูุจูู
  - ุฅุฐุง ุงูุชูู ุงูุฏุนู: ุนุฏู ุงูุดุญู

- 6.2.4: ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุนูููุงุช
  - ุชุณุฌูู ูู ุนูููุฉ ุดุญู
  - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฃุฎุทุงุก ูุงูุชุญุฐูุฑุงุช
  - ุฅูุดุงุก ุชูุฑูุฑ ูููู

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
from apscheduler.schedulers.background import BackgroundScheduler

# ูููุฉ ูุฌุฏููุฉ: ุดุญู ุงูุญุตุต ุงููุฏุนููุฉ
def charge_monthly_subsidies():
    """
    ุชุนูู ูู ุฃูู ููู ูู ูู ุดูุฑ (12:01 ุตุจุงุญุงู)
    ุดุญู ุฌููุน ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงููุฏุนููุฉ ุจุญุตุชูุง ุงูุดูุฑูุฉ
    """
    
    logger.info("ุจุฏุก ุนูููุฉ ุดุญู ุงูุญุตุต ุงููุฏุนููุฉ...")
    
    # ุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู ุงููุดุทูู
    subsidized_subscribers = Subscriber.query.join(
        SubscriberSubsidy
    ).filter(
        SubscriberSubsidy.is_subsidized == True,
        SubscriberSubsidy.subsidy_end_date >= datetime.now().date()
    ).all()
    
    success_count = 0
    error_count = 0
    
    for subscriber in subsidized_subscribers:
        try:
            # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุฏุนู
            subsidy = subscriber.subsidy
            meter = subscriber.meter
            
            if not meter or meter.type != 'smart':
                logger.warning(f"ุงููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id} ูุง ูููู ุนุฏุงุฏ ุฐูู")
                continue
            
            # ุงุณุชุฏุนุงุก API Acrel ูุดุญู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ
            quota = subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh
            
            result = acrel_client.set_monthly_quota(
                device_id=meter.acrel_device_id,
                quota_kwh=quota
            )
            
            if result['success']:
                # ุชุณุฌูู ุนูููุฉ ุงูุดุญู
                charge_log = SubsidyChargeLog(
                    subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
                    charge_date=datetime.now(),
                    quota_kwh=quota,
                    status='success',
                    acrel_response=result
                )
                db.session.add(charge_log)
                success_count += 1
                
                logger.info(
                    f"ุชู ุดุญู ุงููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id} ุจู {quota} ูููู"
                )
            else:
                logger.error(
                    f"ูุดู ุดุญู ุงููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id}: {result['error']}"
                )
                error_count += 1
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุดุญู ุงููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id}: {str(e)}")
            error_count += 1
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุชูุฑูุฑ ููุฎุต
    summary = {
        'total': len(subsidized_subscribers),
        'success': success_count,
        'errors': error_count,
        'timestamp': datetime.now()
    }
    
    logger.info(f"ุงูุชูุช ุนูููุฉ ุงูุดุญู: {summary}")
    
    # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ูููุณุคูููู
    send_notification(
        recipients=['admin@station.com'],
        subject='ุชูุฑูุฑ ุดุญู ุงูุญุตุต ุงููุฏุนููุฉ',
        body=f"ุชู ุดุญู {success_count} ุนุฏุงุฏ ุจูุฌุงุญุ {error_count} ุฃุฎุทุงุก"
    )

# ุฌุฏููุฉ ุงููููุฉ
scheduler = BackgroundScheduler()
scheduler.add_job(
    charge_monthly_subsidies,
    'cron',
    day=1,
    hour=0,
    minute=1,
    timezone='Asia/Aden'
)
scheduler.start()
```

```python
from openpyxl import Workbook
from datetime import datetime, date

def generate_subsidy_reports():
    """
    ุชุนูู ูู ุขุฎุฑ ููู ูู ูู ุดูุฑ (11:59 ูุณุงุกู)
    ุฅูุดุงุก ุชูุงุฑูุฑ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ููู ุจุฑูุงูุฌ ุฏุนู
    """
    
    logger.info("ุจุฏุก ุฅูุดุงุก ุชูุงุฑูุฑ ุตูุฏูู ุงูุฏุนู...")
    
    # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุฌููุน ุจุฑุงูุฌ ุงูุฏุนู ุงููุดุทุฉ
    subsidy_programs = SubsidyProgram.query.filter(
        SubsidyProgram.is_active == True
    ).all()
    
    for program in subsidy_programs:
        try:
            # ุฅูุดุงุก ูุตูู Excel ุฌุฏูุฏ
            wb = Workbook()
            ws = wb.active
            ws.title = "ุชูุฑูุฑ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู"
            
            # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฑุคูุณ ุงูุฃุนูุฏุฉ
            headers = [
                'ุงูุฑูู ุงููุฑุฌุนู',
                'ุงุณู ุงููุดุชุฑู',
                'ุงููุฆุฉ',
                'ุงูุงุณุชููุงู (ูููู)',
                'ุงูุณุนุฑ (ุฑูุงู)',
                'ุงูููุงุญุธุงุช'
            ]
            ws.append(headers)
            
            # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุงููุดุชุฑููู ูู ูุฐุง ุงูุจุฑูุงูุฌ
            subscribers = Subscriber.query.join(
                SubscriberSubsidy
            ).filter(
                SubscriberSubsidy.subsidy_program_id == program.id
            ).all()
            
            total_consumption = 0
            total_amount = 0
            
            for subscriber in subscribers:
                subsidy = subscriber.subsidy
                meter = subscriber.meter
                
                # ุฌูุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ูู Acrel
                consumption_data = acrel_client.get_monthly_consumption(
                    meter_id=meter.acrel_device_id,
                    year=datetime.now().year,
                    month=datetime.now().month - 1  # ุงูุดูุฑ ุงููุงุถู
                )
                
                consumption_kwh = consumption_data['total_kwh']
                amount = consumption_kwh * program.unit_price
                
                # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุตู ูููุดุชุฑู
                ws.append([
                    subsidy.subsidy_reference_number,
                    subscriber.name,
                    subsidy.subsidy_category,
                    consumption_kwh,
                    amount,
                    ''
                ])
                
                total_consumption += consumption_kwh
                total_amount += amount
            
            # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุตู ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู
            ws.append([
                '',
                'ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู',
                '',
                total_consumption,
                total_amount,
                ''
            ])
            
            # ุญูุธ ุงูููู
            filename = f"subsidy_report_{program.id}_{date.today().isoformat()}.xlsx"
            filepath = f"/reports/{filename}"
            wb.save(filepath)
            
            # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุงูุชูุฑูุฑ
            send_email(
                to=program.contact_email,
                subject=f"ุชูุฑูุฑ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู - {program.name}",
                body=f"ูุฑุฌู ูุฑุงุฌุนุฉ ุงูุชูุฑูุฑ ุงููุฑูู",
                attachments=[filepath]
            )
            
            # ุชุณุฌูู ูู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
            report_log = SubsidyReportLog(
                program_id=program.id,
                report_date=datetime.now(),
                filename=filename,
                total_consumption=total_consumption,
                total_amount=total_amount,
                status='sent'
            )
            db.session.add(report_log)
            
            logger.info(
                f"ุชู ุฅูุดุงุก ุชูุฑูุฑ {program.name}: {total_consumption} ูููู"
            )
        
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุฅูุดุงุก ุชูุฑูุฑ {program.name}: {str(e)}")
    
    db.session.commit()

# ุฌุฏููุฉ ุงููููุฉ
scheduler.add_job(
    generate_subsidy_reports,
    'cron',
    day=28,  # ูุจู ููุงูุฉ ุงูุดูุฑ ุจููููู
    hour=23,
    minute=59,
    timezone='Asia/Aden'
)
```

### 6.4: ุฏูุฌ ุขููุฉ ุงูุดุญู ุงูุฅุถุงูู

**ุงููุตู:** ุงูุณูุงุญ ูููุดุชุฑู ุงููุฏุนูู ุจุดุฑุงุก ุฑุตูุฏ ุฅุถุงูู ุนูุฏ ุงูุญุงุฌุฉ.

- 6.4.2: ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุฏูุน ุงูุฅุถุงูู
  - ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุทูุจ ุงูุดุญู ุงูุฅุถุงูู

- 6.4.3: ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุญุตุฉ
  - ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุงูุฑุตูุฏ ุงูุฅุถุงูู ููุนุฏุงุฏ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุณุฌูุงุช
  - ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ูููุดุชุฑู

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
@app.route('/api/subscribers/<id>/charge-additional', methods=['POST'])
def charge_additional_credit(id):
    """
    ุงูุณูุงุญ ูููุดุชุฑู ุงููุฏุนูู ุจุดุฑุงุก ุฑุตูุฏ ุฅุถุงูู
    """
    
    subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(id)
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุฃู ุงููุดุชุฑู ูุฏุนูู
    if not subscriber.subsidy or not subscriber.subsidy.is_subsidized:
        return {'error': 'ุงููุดุชุฑู ุบูุฑ ูุฏุนูู'}, 400
    
    # ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงูุฏูุน
    amount = data.get('amount')
    payment_method = data.get('payment_method')
    
    payment = process_payment(
        subscriber_id=id,
        amount=amount,
        payment_method=payment_method,
        type='additional_credit'
    )
    
    if not payment['success']:
        return {'error': 'ูุดู ุงูุฏูุน'}, 400
    
    # ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุฑุตูุฏ ุงูุฅุถุงูู (ูููููุงุท/ุณุงุนุฉ)
    unit_price = 0.5  # ุฑูุงู ููู ูููู (ูุซุงู)
    additional_kwh = amount / unit_price
    
    # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุดุญู ุฅูู Acrel
    meter = subscriber.meter
    result = acrel_client.add_credit(
        device_id=meter.acrel_device_id,
        credit_kwh=additional_kwh
    )
    
    if result['success']:
        # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุนูููุฉ
        charge_log = AdditionalChargeLog(
            subscriber_id=id,
            amount=amount,
            credit_kwh=additional_kwh,
            payment_id=payment['id'],
            status='success'
        )
        db.session.add(charge_log)
        db.session.commit()
        
        # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ
        send_sms(
            phone=subscriber.phone,
            message=f"ุชู ุดุญู ุนุฏุงุฏู ุจู {additional_kwh} ูููู ุจูุฌุงุญ"
        )
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'credit_kwh': additional_kwh,
            'message': 'ุชู ุงูุดุญู ุจูุฌุงุญ'
        }, 200
    else:
        return {'error': 'ูุดู ุงูุดุญู ูู Acrel'}, 500
```

## ๐ ุงูุฌุฏูู ุงูุฒููู:

  - ุนุฑุถ ูุนูููุงุช ูู ูุดุชุฑู:

- 7.1.3: ูุคุดุฑุงุช ุจุตุฑูุฉ
  - ุดุฑูุท ุชูุฏู ููุถุญ ูุณุจุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู
  - ุฃููุงู:
    - **ุฃุฎุถุฑ:** < 75% ูู ุงูุญุตุฉ
    - **ุฃุตูุฑ:** 75-90% ูู ุงูุญุตุฉ
    - **ุจุฑุชูุงูู:** 90-100% ูู ุงูุญุตุฉ
    - **ุฃุญูุฑ:** > 100% (ุชุฌุงูุฒ)

- 7.1.4: ูุธุงุฆู ุฅุถุงููุฉ
  - ุชุตููุฉ ุญุณุจ ุงููุฆุฉ
  - ุชุตููุฉ ุญุณุจ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ
  - ุชุตุฏูุฑ ุงูุชูุงุฑูุฑ
  - ุชูุจููุงุช ููุฑูุฉ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
class SubsidyConsumptionLog(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    subscriber_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('subscriber.id'))
    reading_date = db.Column(db.Date)
    consumption_kwh = db.Column(db.Float)
    cumulative_consumption = db.Column(db.Float)
    quota_kwh = db.Column(db.Float)
    remaining_quota = db.Column(db.Float)
    overage_kwh = db.Column(db.Float, default=0)
    consumption_percentage = db.Column(db.Float)
    status = db.Column(db.String(20))  # 'normal', 'warning', 'exceeded'
    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)

# API ููุญุตูู ุนูู ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูููุญุฉ
@app.route('/api/dashboard/subsidy-consumption', methods=['GET'])
def get_subsidy_consumption_dashboard():
    """
    ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุจูุงูุงุช ููุญุฉ ูุฑุงูุจุฉ ุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุฏุนู
    """
    
    # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุฌููุน ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู ุนูู ุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุชูููุฏูุฉ
    subsidized_subscribers = Subscriber.query.join(
        SubscriberSubsidy
    ).filter(
        SubscriberSubsidy.is_subsidized == True,
        Meter.type == 'traditional'
    ).all()
    
    dashboard_data = []
    
    for subscriber in subsidized_subscribers:
        subsidy = subscriber.subsidy
        
        # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุขุฎุฑ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ูุฐุง ุงูุดูุฑ
        current_month_start = datetime.now().replace(day=1)
        latest_reading = SubsidyConsumptionLog.query.filter(
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.subscriber_id == subscriber.id,
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.reading_date >= current_month_start
        ).order_by(
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.reading_date.desc()
        ).first()
        
        if not latest_reading:
            continue
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุณุจ ุงููุฆููุฉ ูุงูุญุงูุฉ
        consumption_percentage = (
            latest_reading.cumulative_consumption / subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh
        ) * 100
        
        if consumption_percentage < 75:
            status = 'normal'
            status_color = 'green'
        elif consumption_percentage < 90:
            status = 'warning'
            status_color = 'yellow'
        elif consumption_percentage < 100:
            status = 'caution'
            status_color = 'orange'
        else:
            status = 'exceeded'
            status_color = 'red'
        
        dashboard_data.append({
            'subscriber_id': subscriber.id,
            'subscriber_name': subscriber.name,
            'subscriber_number': subscriber.account_number,
            'subsidy_category': subsidy.subsidy_category,
            'quota_kwh': subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh,
            'current_consumption': latest_reading.cumulative_consumption,
            'remaining_quota': latest_reading.remaining_quota,
            'overage_kwh': latest_reading.overage_kwh,
            'consumption_percentage': round(consumption_percentage, 2),
            'status': status,
            'status_color': status_color,
            'last_reading_date': latest_reading.reading_date.isoformat()
        })
    
    return {
        'total_subscribers': len(dashboard_data),
        'normal': len([d for d in dashboard_data if d['status'] == 'normal']),
        'warning': len([d for d in dashboard_data if d['status'] == 'warning']),
        'caution': len([d for d in dashboard_data if d['status'] == 'caution']),
        'exceeded': len([d for d in dashboard_data if d['status'] == 'exceeded']),
        'data': dashboard_data
    }, 200
```

---

### 7.2: ูุธุงู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช ุงูุงุณุชุจุงููุฉ (Proactive Notification System)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุธุงู ุชููุงุฆู ูุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช ูููุดุชุฑู ูุงูููุธููู ูุจู ูุจุนุฏ ุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 7.2.1: ุจุฑูุฌุฉ ูููุฉ ูุฌุฏููุฉ ููููุฉ
  - ุชุนูู ูู ููู ุงูุณุงุนุฉ 6 ุตุจุงุญุงู
  - ุชูุญุต ุงุณุชููุงู ุฌููุน ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู
  - ุชุญุฏุฏ ูู ูุตู ุฅูู 90% ูู ุงูุญุตุฉ
  - ุชุญุฏุฏ ูู ุชุฌุงูุฒ ุงูุญุตุฉ

- 7.2.2: ุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช ุงูุชุฑุงุจ ุงูุชูุงุก ุงูุญุตุฉ (90%)
  - **ูููุดุชุฑู:** ุฑุณุงูุฉ SMS/WhatsApp
  - **ุงููุญุชูู:** "ุนููููุง ุงูุนุฒูุฒุ ููุฏ ุงุณุชูููุช 90% ูู ุญุตุชู ุงููุฏุนููุฉ. ุฃู ุงุณุชููุงู ุฅุถุงูู ุณูุชู ุงุญุชุณุงุจู ุจุงูุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฌุงุฑู."
  - **ุงููุฏู:** ุชูุจูู ูุณุจู ูุจู ุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ

- 7.2.3: ุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช ุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ (> 100%)
  - **ูููุดุชุฑู:** ุฑุณุงูุฉ SMS/WhatsApp ููุฑูุฉ
  - **ุงููุญุชูู:** "ุนููููุง ุงูุนุฒูุฒุ ููุฏ ุชุฌุงูุฒุช ุญุตุชู ุงููุฏุนููุฉ. ุฑุตูุฏู ุงูุญุงูู: -15 ูููู. ูุฑุฌู ุฒูุงุฑุฉ ุงููููุน ุฃู ุงูุงุชุตุงู ุจูุง ูุชุณููุฉ ุงููุจูุบ."
  - **ุงููุฏู:** ุฅุจูุงุบ ููุฑู ุจุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ ูุน ุฑูุงุจุท ุงูุฏูุน

- 7.2.4: ุชูุจููุงุช ุฏุงุฎููุฉ ููููุธููู
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ููุญุฉ ุงููุฑุงูุจุฉ ููุฑุงู
  - ุฅุฑุณุงู ุชูุจูู ุจุฑูุฏู ูููุฏูุฑ
  - ุชุณุฌูู ูู ุณุฌู ุงูุฃุญุฏุงุซ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
def check_and_notify_subsidy_status():
    """
    ูููุฉ ูุฌุฏููุฉ ููููุฉ: ูุญุต ุงุณุชููุงู ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู
    ูุฅุฑุณุงู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช ุงูููุงุณุจุฉ
    """
    
    logger.info("ุจุฏุก ูุญุต ุญุงูุฉ ุงุณุชููุงู ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู...")
    
    # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุฌููุน ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู ุนูู ุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุชูููุฏูุฉ
    subsidized_subscribers = Subscriber.query.join(
        SubscriberSubsidy
    ).filter(
        SubscriberSubsidy.is_subsidized == True,
        Meter.type == 'traditional'
    ).all()
    
    notifications_sent = 0
    
    for subscriber in subsidized_subscribers:
        subsidy = subscriber.subsidy
        
        # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุขุฎุฑ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ูุฐุง ุงูุดูุฑ
        current_month_start = datetime.now().replace(day=1)
        latest_reading = SubsidyConsumptionLog.query.filter(
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.subscriber_id == subscriber.id,
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.reading_date >= current_month_start
        ).order_by(
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.reading_date.desc()
        ).first()
        
        if not latest_reading:
            continue
        
        consumption_percentage = (
            latest_reading.cumulative_consumption / subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh
        ) * 100
        
        # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุญุงูุฉ ุงูุณุงุจูุฉ
        previous_status = NotificationLog.query.filter(
            NotificationLog.subscriber_id == subscriber.id,
            NotificationLog.notification_type.in_(['warning_90', 'exceeded'])
        ).order_by(
            NotificationLog.created_at.desc()
        ).first()
        
        # ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ุงูุชุฑุงุจ ุงูุชูุงุก ุงูุญุตุฉ (90%)
        if 90 <= consumption_percentage < 100:
            if not previous_status or previous_status.notification_type != 'warning_90':
                # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ
                message = f"ุนููููุง ุงูุนุฒูุฒุ ููุฏ ุงุณุชูููุช {consumption_percentage:.1f}% ูู ุญุตุชู ุงููุฏุนููุฉ ({subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh} ูููู). ุฃู ุงุณุชููุงู ุฅุถุงูู ุณูุชู ุงุญุชุณุงุจู ุจุงูุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฌุงุฑู."
                
                send_sms(subscriber.phone, message)
                send_whatsapp(subscriber.phone, message)
                
                # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑ
                notification_log = NotificationLog(
                    subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
                    notification_type='warning_90',
                    message=message,
                    status='sent'
                )
                db.session.add(notification_log)
                notifications_sent += 1
                
                logger.info(f"ุชู ุฅุฑุณุงู ุชูุจูู 90% ูููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id}")
        
        # ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ (> 100%)
        elif consumption_percentage > 100:
            if not previous_status or previous_status.notification_type != 'exceeded':
                # ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุจูุบ ุงููุชุฌุงูุฒ
                overage_kwh = latest_reading.cumulative_consumption - subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh
                overage_amount = overage_kwh * 0.5  # ุงูุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฌุงุฑู (ูุซุงู)
                
                # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ
                message = f"ุนููููุง ุงูุนุฒูุฒุ ููุฏ ุชุฌุงูุฒุช ุญุตุชู ุงููุฏุนููุฉ. ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุฅุถุงูู: {overage_kwh:.1f} ูููู ({overage_amount:.2f} ุฑูุงู). ูุฑุฌู ุงูุฏูุน ูุชุฌูุจ ูุทุน ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ. ุงูุฑุงุจุท: [payment_link]"
                
                send_sms(subscriber.phone, message)
                send_whatsapp(subscriber.phone, message)
                
                # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑ
                notification_log = NotificationLog(
                    subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
                    notification_type='exceeded',
                    message=message,
                    status='sent',
                    overage_kwh=overage_kwh,
                    overage_amount=overage_amount
                )
                db.session.add(notification_log)
                notifications_sent += 1
                
                # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุชูุจูู ุฏุงุฎูู ููููุธููู
                send_internal_alert(
                    recipients=['manager@station.com'],
                    subject=f'ุชุฌุงูุฒ ุฏุนู: {subscriber.name}',
                    body=f'ุงููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.name} ุชุฌุงูุฒ ุญุตุชู ุจู {overage_kwh:.1f} ูููู'
                )
                
                logger.warning(f"ุชุฌุงูุฒ ุฏุนู ูููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id}: {overage_kwh:.1f} ูููู")
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    logger.info(f"ุงูุชูู ุงููุญุต: ุชู ุฅุฑุณุงู {notifications_sent} ุฅุดุนุงุฑ")

# ุฌุฏููุฉ ุงููููุฉ
scheduler.add_job(
    check_and_notify_subsidy_status,
    'cron',
    hour=6,
    minute=0,
    timezone='Asia/Aden'
)
```

### 7.3: ุชูููู ูุธุงู ุงูููุชุฑุฉ ููุชุนุงูู ูุน ุงูุฏููู

**ุงููุตู:** ุชุนุฏูู ูุธุงู ุงูููุชุฑุฉ ููุตู ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงููุฏุนูู ุนู ุงููุฏููููุฉ.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 7.3.1: ูุตู ุงูุงุณุชููุงู
  - ุงูุฌุฒุก ุงููุฏุนูู (ุญุชู 82 ุฃู 64 ูููู)
  - ุงูุฌุฒุก ุงูุฅุถุงูู (ุงูุชุฌุงูุฒ)

- 7.3.2: ุฅูุดุงุก ููุงุชูุฑ ูููุตูุฉ
  - ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ููุตูุฏูู: ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงููุฏุนูู ููุท
  - ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ูููุดุชุฑู: ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุฅุถุงูู

- 7.3.3: ุชุชุจุน ุงููุฏููููุฉ
  - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฏููู ูู ููู ุงููุดุชุฑู
  - ุนุฑุถ ุงูุฏููู ุงููุชุฑุงููุฉ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุฏููู ุนูุฏ ุงูุฏูุน

- 7.3.4: ุชูุงุฑูุฑ ุงูุฏููู
  - ุชูุฑูุฑ ูููู ุจุงูุฏููู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
  - ุชูุฑูุฑ ุฃุณุจูุนู ุจุงูุฏููู ุงููุชุฑุงููุฉ
  - ุชูุฑูุฑ ุดูุฑู ุจุฅุฌูุงูู ุงูุฏููู

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
def generate_end_of_month_invoices():
    """
    ูู ููุงูุฉ ุงูุดูุฑ: ุฅูุดุงุก ููุงุชูุฑ ูููุตูุฉ ููุงุณุชููุงู ุงููุฏุนูู ูุงูุฅุถุงูู
    """
    
    logger.info("ุจุฏุก ุฅูุดุงุก ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ุงูุดูุฑูุฉ...")
    
    current_month_start = datetime.now().replace(day=1)
    current_month_end = (current_month_start + timedelta(days=32)).replace(day=1) - timedelta(days=1)
    
    # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุฌููุน ุงููุดุชุฑููู ุงููุฏุนูููู ุนูู ุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุชูููุฏูุฉ
    subsidized_subscribers = Subscriber.query.join(
        SubscriberSubsidy
    ).filter(
        SubscriberSubsidy.is_subsidized == True,
        Meter.type == 'traditional'
    ).all()
    
    for subscriber in subsidized_subscribers:
        subsidy = subscriber.subsidy
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููู ูุฐุง ุงูุดูุฑ
        total_consumption = SubsidyConsumptionLog.query.filter(
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.subscriber_id == subscriber.id,
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.reading_date >= current_month_start,
            SubsidyConsumptionLog.reading_date <= current_month_end
        ).with_entities(
            db.func.sum(SubsidyConsumptionLog.consumption_kwh)
        ).scalar() or 0
        
        # ูุตู ุงูุงุณุชููุงู
        subsidized_consumption = min(total_consumption, subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh)
        additional_consumption = max(0, total_consumption - subsidy.monthly_quota_kwh)
        
        # 1. ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ููุตูุฏูู (ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงููุฏุนูู ููุท)
        subsidy_invoice = Invoice(
            subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
            invoice_type='subsidy',
            period_start=current_month_start,
            period_end=current_month_end,
            consumption_kwh=subsidized_consumption,
            unit_price=0,  # ูุฌุงูู (ูุฏูุนู ุงูุตูุฏูู)
            total_amount=0,
            status='pending',
            recipient='subsidy_fund'
        )
        db.session.add(subsidy_invoice)
        
        # 2. ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ูููุดุชุฑู (ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุฅุถุงูู ููุท)
        if additional_consumption > 0:
            additional_amount = additional_consumption * 0.5  # ุงูุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฌุงุฑู
            
            additional_invoice = Invoice(
                subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
                invoice_type='additional',
                period_start=current_month_start,
                period_end=current_month_end,
                consumption_kwh=additional_consumption,
                unit_price=0.5,
                total_amount=additional_amount,
                status='unpaid',
                recipient='subscriber'
            )
            db.session.add(additional_invoice)
            
            # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงููุฏููููุฉ
            debt_record = SubscriberDebt(
                subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
                invoice_id=additional_invoice.id,
                amount=additional_amount,
                reason='subsidy_overage',
                due_date=current_month_end + timedelta(days=15),
                status='unpaid'
            )
            db.session.add(debt_record)
            
            logger.info(
                f"ุงููุดุชุฑู {subscriber.id}: ุงุณุชููุงู ุฅุถุงูู {additional_consumption} ููููุ ุฏูู {additional_amount} ุฑูุงู"
            )
    
    db.session.commit()
    logger.info("ุงูุชูุช ุนูููุฉ ุฅูุดุงุก ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ุงูุดูุฑูุฉ")

# ุฌุฏููุฉ ุงููููุฉ
scheduler.add_job(
    generate_end_of_month_invoices,
    'cron',
    day=28,
    hour=23,
    minute=59,
    timezone='Asia/Aden'
)
```

## ๐ ูุณุงุฑ ุงูุชุฑุญูู ุงููุณุชูุจูู:

ูุฐุง ุงูุญู ูููุฑ **ูุณุงุฑ ูุงุถุญ ููุชุฑุญูู** ุฅูู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงูุฐููุฉ:

## ๐ฏ ุงููุฏู:

ุจูุงุก ูุธุงู ุดุงูู ูุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูู ูุชุชุจุน ุฌููุน ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงูุฎุงุถุนุฉ ููุฑูุงุจุฉ (ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุชุ ุงูุฃุฎุชุงูุ ุงูููุงุทุนุ ุงูุฃุณูุงู) ูู ุงูุดุฑุงุก ุฅูู ุงูุชุฑููุจ ูุงูุชูุงุนุฏ.

### ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุฎุฒููุฉ ุงููุทููุจุฉ:

| ุงูุตูู | ููุน ุงูุชุชุจุน | ุงูุฃูููุฉ | ุงูููุงุญุธุงุช |

### ุงูุชุญุฏูุงุช ุงูุญุงููุฉ:
- โ ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ุฑุคูุฉ ููุญุฏุฉ ูููุฎุฒูู
- โ ุงูุฃุฎุชุงู ูุงูููุงุทุน ูุง ุชูุชุจุน ุจุฏูุฉ
- โ ุตุนูุจุฉ ูู ุชุชุจุน ุงูุฃุตูู ุจุนุฏ ุงูุชุฑููุจ
- โ ุนูููุงุช ูุฏููุฉ ูุนูุฏุฉ ูุนุฑุถุฉ ููุฃุฎุทุงุก
- โ ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ุฑูุงุจุฉ ุนูู ุงูุงุญุชูุงู

## ๐ ุงูููุงู ุงููุฑุนูุฉ:

### 8.1: ูุชุงููุฌ ุงูุฃุตูุงู (Item Catalog)

**ุงููุตู:** ุชุนุฑูู ุฌููุน ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุฎุฒููุฉ ูุฎุตุงุฆุตูุง.

**ุงูููุงู:**

  - `description`: ูุตู ููุตู

- 8.1.2: ูุงุฌูุฉ ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฃุตูุงู ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
  - ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุนุฏุงุฏ ุฌุฏูุฏ (ููุนุ ุณุนุฉุ ุณุนุฑ)

- 8.1.3: ุชูุงุฑูุฑ ุงูุฃุตูุงู
  - ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุดุทุฉ
  - ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุชูุงุนุฏุฉ
  - ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงูุชู ุชุญุชุงุฌ ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุทูุจ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**

```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
class InventoryItem(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    item_code = db.Column(db.String(50), unique=True)
    item_name = db.Column(db.String(200))
    item_category = db.Column(db.String(50))  # 'meter', 'seal', 'breaker', 'wire'
    tracking_type = db.Column(db.String(20))  # 'serial', 'quantity'
    unit_price = db.Column(db.Float)
    supplier_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('supplier.id'))
    reorder_level = db.Column(db.Integer)
    current_stock = db.Column(db.Integer, default=0)
    description = db.Column(db.Text)
    is_active = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=True)
    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)

# API ูุฅุถุงูุฉ ุตูู ุฌุฏูุฏ
@app.route('/api/inventory/items', methods=['POST'])
def create_inventory_item():
    data = request.json
    
    item = InventoryItem(
        item_code=data['item_code'],
        item_name=data['item_name'],
        item_category=data['category'],
        tracking_type=data['tracking_type'],
        unit_price=data['unit_price'],
        supplier_id=data['supplier_id'],
        reorder_level=data['reorder_level'],
        description=data.get('description')
    )
    
    db.session.add(item)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {'status': 'success', 'item_id': item.id}, 201
```

### 8.2: ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูู ุงููุชูุฏูุฉ (Advanced Inventory Management)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุธุงู ูุชูุฏู ูุชุชุจุน ูู ูุทุนุฉ ุนูู ุญุฏุฉ.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 8.2.1: ุฌุฏูู ุชุชุจุน ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุฑุฏูุฉ
  - `unit_id`: ูุนุฑูู ูุฑูุฏ ููู ูุทุนุฉ
  - `item_id`: ุงูุตูู
  - `serial_number`: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุณูู
  - `status`: ุงูุญุงูุฉ (in_stock, issued, installed, retired)
  - `location`: ุงููููุน ุงูุญุงูู
  - `assigned_to`: ูู ูููููุง ุญุงููุงู
  - `installation_date`: ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงูุชุฑููุจ
  - `installed_at_subscriber`: ุฑูู ุงููุดุชุฑู

- 8.2.2: ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุงููุฎุฒูู
  - ูุณุญ ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุณููุฉ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุญุงูุฉ ุฅูู "ูู ุงููุฎุฒู"
  - ุฅูุดุงุก ูููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจูุฉ ุชููุงุฆูุฉ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ูุณุชููุงุช ุงููุฎุฒูู

- 8.2.3: ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุตุฑู ูู ุงููุฎุฒูู
  - ุงุฎุชูุงุฑ ุงูุตูู ูุงููููุฉ
  - ูุณุญ ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุตููุฉ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุญุงูุฉ ุฅูู "ูุน ุงููุญุทุฉ"
  - ุชุณุฌูู ุงููุณุคูู ุนู ุงูุตุฑู

- 8.2.4: ุชูุงุฑูุฑ ุงููุฎุฒูู
  - ุงููุฎุฒูู ุงูุญุงูู ุจุงูุชูุตูู
  - ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงูุชู ุชุญุชุงุฌ ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุทูุจ
  - ุญุฑูุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูู (In/Out)
  - ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงูููููุฏุฉ ุฃู ุงููุชุฃุฎุฑุฉ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
class InventoryUnit(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    unit_code = db.Column(db.String(100), unique=True)
    item_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('inventory_item.id'))
    serial_number = db.Column(db.String(100), unique=True)
    status = db.Column(db.String(20))  # 'in_stock', 'issued', 'installed', 'retired'
    location = db.Column(db.String(100))
    assigned_to = db.Column(db.String(100))  # station name or person
    installation_date = db.Column(db.Date)
    installed_at_subscriber_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('subscriber.id'))
    received_date = db.Column(db.DateTime)
    issued_date = db.Column(db.DateTime)
    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)

# API ูุงุณุชูุจุงู ูุฎุฒูู ุฌุฏูุฏ
@app.route('/api/inventory/receive', methods=['POST'])
def receive_inventory():
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - item_id: ูุนุฑูู ุงูุตูู
    # - serial_numbers: ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุณููุฉ
    # - purchase_order_id: ุฑูู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุดุฑุงุก
    
    item = InventoryItem.query.get(data['item_id'])
    serial_numbers = data['serial_numbers']
    
    created_units = []
    total_amount = 0
    
    for serial in serial_numbers:
        unit = InventoryUnit(
            unit_code=f"{item.item_code}-{serial}",
            item_id=item.id,
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock',
            location='Main Warehouse',
            received_date=datetime.now()
        )
        db.session.add(unit)
        created_units.append(unit)
        total_amount += item.unit_price
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ูุณุชูู ุงููุฎุฒูู
    item.current_stock += len(serial_numbers)
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจู ุชููุงุฆู
    journal_entry = JournalEntry(
        entry_date=datetime.now(),
        description=f"ุงุณุชูุจุงู {len(serial_numbers)} ร {item.item_name}",
        debit_account='Inventory',
        debit_amount=total_amount,
        credit_account='Accounts Payable',
        credit_amount=total_amount,
        reference_id=data.get('purchase_order_id'),
        reference_type='purchase_order'
    )
    db.session.add(journal_entry)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'units_received': len(created_units),
        'total_amount': total_amount,
        'journal_entry_id': journal_entry.id
    }, 201

# API ูุตุฑู ูุฎุฒูู
@app.route('/api/inventory/issue', methods=['POST'])
def issue_inventory():
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - item_id: ูุนุฑูู ุงูุตูู
    # - serial_numbers: ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุตููุฉ
    # - station_id: ุงููุญุทุฉ ุงููุณุชูุจูุฉ
    # - issued_by: ูู ูุงู ุจุงูุตุฑู
    
    station = Station.query.get(data['station_id'])
    issued_units = []
    
    for serial in data['serial_numbers']:
        unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        
        if not unit:
            return {'error': f'ุงููุญุฏุฉ {serial} ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏุฉ ุฃู ูุตุฑููุฉ'}, 400
        
        unit.status = 'issued'
        unit.assigned_to = station.name
        unit.location = f"Station: {station.name}"
        unit.issued_date = datetime.now()
        
        issued_units.append(unit)
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'units_issued': len(issued_units),
        'assigned_to': station.name
    }, 200
```

### 8.3: ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุฃูุงูุฑ ุงูุดุฑุงุก (Purchase Order Management)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุธุงู ูุชูุงูู ูุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุนูููุงุช ุงูุดุฑุงุก.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 8.3.1: ุฅูุดุงุก ุฃูุฑ ุดุฑุงุก
  - ุงุฎุชูุงุฑ ุงูุตูู ูุงููููุฉ
  - ุงุฎุชูุงุฑ ุงูููุฑุฏ
  - ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุจูุบ ุชููุงุฆูุงู
  - ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจู (ูุฏูู: ูุดุชุฑูุงุชุ ุฏุงุฆู: ููุฏูุฉ)

- 8.3.2: ุชุชุจุน ุฃูุฑ ุงูุดุฑุงุก
  - ุญุงูุงุช: ูุณูุฏุฉุ ูุฑุณูุ ููุฏ ุงูุงุณุชูุจุงูุ ูุณุชูุจู
  - ุชูุจููุงุช ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุฃุฎูุฑ
  - ุชูุงุฑูุฑ ุงูุฃูุงูุฑ ุงููุนููุฉ

- 8.3.3: ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุดุฑุงุก
  - ูุทุงุจูุฉ ุงููููุฉ ุงููุณุชูุจูุฉ ูุน ุงูุฃูุฑ
  - ูุณุญ ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุตููุฉ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุฃูุฑ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
class PurchaseOrder(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    po_number = db.Column(db.String(50), unique=True)
    supplier_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('supplier.id'))
    item_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('inventory_item.id'))
    quantity = db.Column(db.Integer)
    unit_price = db.Column(db.Float)
    total_amount = db.Column(db.Float)
    status = db.Column(db.String(20))  # 'draft', 'sent', 'pending', 'received'
    order_date = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    expected_delivery = db.Column(db.Date)
    received_date = db.Column(db.Date)
    received_quantity = db.Column(db.Integer, default=0)
    created_by = db.Column(db.String(100))
    notes = db.Column(db.Text)

# API ูุฅูุดุงุก ุฃูุฑ ุดุฑุงุก
@app.route('/api/purchase-orders', methods=['POST'])
def create_purchase_order():
    data = request.json
    
    item = InventoryItem.query.get(data['item_id'])
    supplier = Supplier.query.get(data['supplier_id'])
    
    total_amount = item.unit_price * data['quantity']
    
    po = PurchaseOrder(
        po_number=generate_po_number(),
        supplier_id=supplier.id,
        item_id=item.id,
        quantity=data['quantity'],
        unit_price=item.unit_price,
        total_amount=total_amount,
        status='draft',
        expected_delivery=data.get('expected_delivery'),
        created_by=current_user.username,
        notes=data.get('notes')
    )
    
    db.session.add(po)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'po_id': po.id,
        'po_number': po.po_number,
        'total_amount': total_amount
    }, 201
```

### 8.4: ุชุทุจูู ุงูููู ุงูููุฏุงูู (Field Technician App)

  - ุชุตููุฉ ุญุณุจ ุงูุญุงูุฉ ูุงููููุน

  - ุชุฃููุฏ ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ููุฎุชู

- 8.4.3: ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุญุงูุฉ

  - ุฅุฑุณุงู ุชุญุฏูุซุงุช ููุฑูุฉ ููุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ

- 8.4.4: ุงูุชูููุน ุงูุฑููู
  - ุชูููุน ุงูุนููู ุนูู ุฅูุฌุงุฒ ุงูุนูู
  - ุชูููุน ุงูููู ุนูู ุงููุณุคูููุฉ
  - ุญูุธ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงูููุซูุฉ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
# API ูุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุชุฑููุจ
@app.route('/api/installation/<installation_id>/complete', methods=['POST'])
def complete_installation(installation_id):
    data = request.json
    
    installation = Installation.query.get(installation_id)
    
    # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุตููุฉ
    meter_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['meter_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    seal_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['seal_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    breaker_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['breaker_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    if not all([meter_unit, seal_unit, breaker_unit]):
        return {'error': 'ุฃุญุฏ ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุบูุฑ ุตุญูุญ'}, 400
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุฃุตูุงู
    meter_unit.status = 'installed'
    meter_unit.installed_at_subscriber_id = installation.subscriber_id
    meter_unit.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    seal_unit.status = 'installed'
    seal_unit.installed_at_subscriber_id = installation.subscriber_id
    seal_unit.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    breaker_unit.status = 'installed'
    breaker_unit.installed_at_subscriber_id = installation.subscriber_id
    breaker_unit.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุชุฑููุจ
    installation.status = 'completed'
    installation.completion_date = datetime.now()
    installation.meter_serial = data['meter_serial']
    installation.seal_serial = data['seal_serial']
    installation.breaker_serial = data['breaker_serial']
    installation.breaker_type = data['breaker_type']
    installation.seal_color = data['seal_color']
    installation.technician_notes = data.get('notes')
    
    # ุญูุธ ุงูุตูุฑ
    if 'photos' in data:
        for photo_data in data['photos']:
            photo = InstallationPhoto(
                installation_id=installation.id,
                photo_url=save_photo(photo_data),
                photo_type=photo_data.get('type')  # 'meter', 'installation', 'overall'
            )
            db.session.add(photo)
    
    # ุชูุนูู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ูู ูุธุงู ุงูููุชุฑุฉ
    meter = installation.meter
    meter.is_active = True
    meter.activation_date = datetime.now()
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'installation_id': installation.id,
        'meter_activated': True,
        'completion_date': installation.completion_date.isoformat()
    }, 200
```

```python
class MaintenanceWorkOrder(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    work_order_number = db.Column(db.String(50), unique=True)
    subscriber_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('subscriber.id'))
    request_type = db.Column(db.String(50))  # 'maintenance', 'replacement', 'upgrade'
    reason = db.Column(db.String(500))
    priority = db.Column(db.String(20))  # 'urgent', 'high', 'normal', 'low'
    status = db.Column(db.String(20))  # 'new', 'assigned', 'in_progress', 'completed'
    assigned_technician_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('technician.id'))
    created_date = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    assigned_date = db.Column(db.DateTime)
    completed_date = db.Column(db.DateTime)
    notes = db.Column(db.Text)
    created_by = db.Column(db.String(100))

# API ูุฅูุดุงุก ุทูุจ ุตูุงูุฉ
@app.route('/api/maintenance/work-orders', methods=['POST'])
def create_work_order():
    data = request.json
    
    subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(data['subscriber_id'])
    
    # ุฌูุจ ุงูููููุงุช ุงูุญุงููุฉ
    current_components = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        installed_at_subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
        status='installed'
    ).all()
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder(
        work_order_number=generate_wo_number(),
        subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
        request_type=data['request_type'],
        reason=data['reason'],
        priority=data.get('priority', 'normal'),
        status='new',
        notes=data.get('notes'),
        created_by=current_user.username
    )
    
    db.session.add(work_order)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'work_order_id': work_order.id,
        'work_order_number': work_order.work_order_number,
        'current_components': [
            {
                'type': unit.item.item_category,
                'serial_number': unit.serial_number,
                'installed_date': unit.installation_date.isoformat()
            }
            for unit in current_components
        ]
    }, 201

# API ูุฅุณูุงุฏ ุทูุจ ุตูุงูุฉ
@app.route('/api/maintenance/work-orders/<wo_id>/assign', methods=['PUT'])
def assign_work_order(wo_id):
    data = request.json
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(wo_id)
    technician = Technician.query.get(data['technician_id'])
    
    work_order.assigned_technician_id = technician.id
    work_order.status = 'assigned'
    work_order.assigned_date = datetime.now()
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ููููู
    send_notification(
        recipient=technician.phone,
        message=f"ุชู ุฅุณูุงุฏ ุทูุจ ุตูุงูุฉ ุฌุฏูุฏ: {work_order.work_order_number}",
        type='sms'
    )
    
    return {'status': 'success'}, 200
```

### 9.2: ุชุญุฏูุซ ุชุทุจูู ุงูููู ุงูููุฏุงูู (Field Technician App Enhancement)

- 9.2.1: ูุงุฆูุฉ ุทูุจุงุช ุงูุตูุงูุฉ
  - ุนุฑุถ ุฌููุน ุงูุทูุจุงุช ุงููุณูุฏุฉ

- 9.2.2: ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
  - ุนุฑุถ ุงูููููุงุช ุงูุญุงููุฉ ุงููุฑูุจุฉ
  - ุฎูุงุฑ "ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู" ุจุฌุงูุจ ูู ูููู
  - ูุณุญ ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ูููููู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ
  - ูุณุญ ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ูููููู ุงููุฏูู
  - ุฅุถุงูุฉ ููุงุญุธุงุช ุญูู ุงูุณุจุจ

- 9.2.3: ุชูุซูู ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
  - ุงูุชูุงุท ุตูุฑ ูุจู ูุจุนุฏ
  - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูููุช ุงููุณุชุบุฑู
  - ุชูููุน ุงูุนููู

- 9.2.4: ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูู ุงูููุฏุงูู

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
# API ูุชุญุฏูุซ ุงููููู (ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู)
@app.route('/api/maintenance/work-orders/<wo_id>/replace-component', methods=['POST'])
def replace_component(wo_id):
    data = request.json
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(wo_id)
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - component_type: ููุน ุงููููู ('meter', 'seal', 'breaker')
    # - old_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ูููููู ุงููุฏูู
    # - new_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ูููููู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ
    # - reason: ุณุจุจ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
    # - technician_id: ุงูููู
    
    component_type = data['component_type']
    old_serial = data['old_serial']
    new_serial = data['new_serial']
    reason = data['reason']
    
    # ุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุงูููููุงุช
    old_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=old_serial,
        installed_at_subscriber_id=work_order.subscriber_id
    ).first()
    
    new_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=new_serial,
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    if not old_unit or not new_unit:
        return {'error': 'ุฃุญุฏ ุงูููููุงุช ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏ'}, 400
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงููููู ุงููุฏูู
    old_unit.status = 'defective'
    old_unit.installed_at_subscriber_id = None
    old_unit.installation_date = None
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงููููู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ
    new_unit.status = 'installed'
    new_unit.installed_at_subscriber_id = work_order.subscriber_id
    new_unit.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุนูููุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
    replacement_log = ComponentReplacement(
        work_order_id=work_order.id,
        component_type=component_type,
        old_unit_id=old_unit.id,
        new_unit_id=new_unit.id,
        reason=reason,
        technician_id=data['technician_id'],
        replacement_date=datetime.now()
    )
    db.session.add(replacement_log)
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ููู ุงููุดุชุฑู
    subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(work_order.subscriber_id)
    if component_type == 'meter':
        subscriber.meter_serial = new_serial
    elif component_type == 'seal':
        subscriber.seal_serial = new_serial
    elif component_type == 'breaker':
        subscriber.breaker_serial = new_serial
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'replacement_id': replacement_log.id,
        'old_component': old_serial,
        'new_component': new_serial,
        'replacement_date': replacement_log.replacement_date.isoformat()
    }, 200
```

### 9.3: ููุทู ุงูุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุชููุงุฆู (Automatic Update Logic)

**ุงููุตู:** ุชุญุฏูุซ ุฌููุน ุงูุณุฌูุงุช ุชููุงุฆูุงู ุนูุฏ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูููู.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 9.3.1: ุชุญุฏูุซ ููู ุงููุดุชุฑู
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูููููุงุช
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุขุฎุฑ ุตูุงูุฉ
  - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุณุฌู ุงูุชุงุฑูุฎู

- 9.3.2: ุชุญุฏูุซ ุณุฌูุงุช ุงููุฎุฒูู
  - ุชุบููุฑ ุญุงูุฉ ุงููููู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ ุฅูู "ูุฑูุจ"
  - ุชุบููุฑ ุญุงูุฉ ุงููููู ุงููุฏูู ุฅูู "ุชุงูู"
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ูููุน ุงููููู ุงูุชุงูู

- 9.3.3: ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงูุณุฌูุงุช ุงููุญุงุณุจูุฉ
  - ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ุชุญุช ุงูุถูุงู: ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ูุงุชูุฑุฉ
  - ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ุนูู ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุนููู: ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ
  - ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ุนูู ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุตูุงูุฉ: ุชุณุฌูู ูู ุชูุงููู ุงูุตูุงูุฉ

- 9.3.4: ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช
  - ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ููุนููู ุจุฅูุฌุงุฒ ุงูุตูุงูุฉ
  - ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ููุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุจุฅูุฌุงุฒ ุงูุทูุจ
  - ุชุญุฏูุซ ุณุฌู ุงูุฃุญุฏุงุซ

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
def process_maintenance_completion(work_order_id):
    """
    ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุฅููุงู ุทูุจ ุงูุตูุงูุฉ ูุชุญุฏูุซ ุฌููุน ุงูุณุฌูุงุช
    """
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(work_order_id)
    
    # ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุฌููุน ุนูููุงุช ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูู ูุฐุง ุงูุทูุจ
    replacements = ComponentReplacement.query.filter_by(
        work_order_id=work_order_id
    ).all()
    
    total_cost = 0
    
    for replacement in replacements:
        new_unit = InventoryUnit.query.get(replacement.new_unit_id)
        item = new_unit.item
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูููุฉ
        if replacement.reason == 'warranty':
            cost = 0
        else:
            cost = item.unit_price
        
        total_cost += cost
        
        # ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุฅุฐุง ูุฒู ุงูุฃูุฑ
        if cost > 0:
            invoice = Invoice(
                subscriber_id=work_order.subscriber_id,
                invoice_type='maintenance',
                description=f"ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู {item.item_name}",
                amount=cost,
                status='unpaid',
                due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15)
            )
            db.session.add(invoice)
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุทูุจ ุงูุตูุงูุฉ
    work_order.status = 'completed'
    work_order.completed_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ููุนููู
    subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(work_order.subscriber_id)
    send_notification(
        recipient=subscriber.phone,
        message=f"ุชู ุฅูุฌุงุฒ ุทูุจ ุงูุตูุงูุฉ {work_order.work_order_number} ุจูุฌุงุญ",
        type='sms'
    )
    
    # ุฅุฑุณุงู ุฅุดุนุงุฑ ููุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ
    send_internal_notification(
        recipients=['manager@station.com'],
        subject=f'ุฅููุงู ุทูุจ ุตูุงูุฉ: {work_order.work_order_number}',
        body=f'ุชู ุฅูุฌุงุฒ ุงูุทูุจ ููุนููู {subscriber.name}. ุงูุชูููุฉ ุงูุฅุฌูุงููุฉ: {total_cost} ุฑูุงู'
    )
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    logger.info(f"ุชู ุฅููุงู ุทูุจ ุงูุตูุงูุฉ {work_order_id}")
```

# ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุฑุฌ: ุชุชุจุน ุดุงุดุงุช STS (Customer Interface Unit - CIU)
## Critical Update: STS Customer Interface Unit (CIU) Tracking

**ุงูุฃููููุฉ:** ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู  
**ุงูุชุฃุซูุฑ:** ุฌููุน ุงูููุงู ุงูุณุงุจูุฉ (7ุ 8ุ 9)  
**ุงูุญุงูุฉ:** ุชุญุฏูุซ ุดุงูู

---

## ๐ฏ ุงููุฏู:

ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุดุงุดุงุช ุงูุนุฑุถ ุงูุฏุงุฎููุฉ (CIU) ูุฃุตูุงู ูุฎุฒููุฉ ูุน ุชุชุจุน ุชุณูุตูู ูุงููุ ูู ุงูุดุฑุงุก ุฅูู ุงูุชุณููู ููุนููู ุฅูู ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู.

---

## ๐ ุงูุณูุงู:

### ูุง ูู ุดุงุดุฉ STS (CIU)ุ
- **Customer Interface Unit:** ูุญุฏุฉ ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุนููู
- **ุงููุธููุฉ:** ุนุฑุถ ุงูุฑุตูุฏ ุงููุชุจูู ูุงูุงุณุชููุงู
- **ุงูููููุฉ:** ุชุณููู ููุนููู (ููุณุช ูู ุงููุญุทุฉ)
- **ุงูุฃูููุฉ:** ุฃุตู ูุงุฏู ูุฌุจ ุชุชุจุนู

### ุงูุชุญุฏูุงุช:
- โ ุงูุดุงุดุงุช ูุฏ ุชุชุนุทู ุฃู ุชุถูุน
- โ ูุฌุจ ุชุชุจุน ูู ูููู ูู ุดุงุดุฉ
- โ ูุฏ ุชุญุชุงุฌ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูููุตู ุนู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ
- โ ูุฌุจ ุชูุซูู ุชุณููููุง ููุนููู

---

## ๐ ุงูุชุญุฏูุซุงุช ุงููุทููุจุฉ:

### ุชุญุฏูุซ 7.1: ูุชุงููุฌ ุงูุฃุตูุงู (ูุญุฏูุซ)

**ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุตูู ุฌุฏูุฏ:**

```python
# ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุตูู ุดุงุดุฉ STS
sts_screen_item = InventoryItem(
    item_code='STS-CIU-001',
    item_name='ุดุงุดุฉ ุนุฑุถ STS (CIU)',
    item_category='sts_screen',
    tracking_type='serial',
    unit_price=150.00,
    supplier_id=supplier_acrel.id,
    reorder_level=50,
    description='ูุญุฏุฉ ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุนููู ูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช STS - ุชุณููู ููุนููู'
)
db.session.add(sts_screen_item)
```

**ุงูุฎุตุงุฆุต ุงููุฑูุฏุฉ:**
- `item_category`: 'sts_screen'
- `tracking_type`: 'serial' (ุฑูู ุชุณูุตูู ูุฑูุฏ)
- `customer_property`: True (ููู ุงูุนููู)
- `returnable`: True (ูุงุจูุฉ ููุงุณุชุฑุฌุงุน ุนูุฏ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู)

---

### ุชุญุฏูุซ 7.2: ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูู (ูุญุฏูุซ)

**ุนูุฏ ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุนุฏุงุฏุงุช STS:**

```python
@app.route('/api/inventory/receive-sts-bundle', methods=['POST'])
def receive_sts_bundle():
    """
    ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุญุฒูุฉ STS ูุงููุฉ:
    - ุนุฏุงุฏ STS
    - ุดุงุดุฉ ุนุฑุถ (CIU)
    - ุฎุชู
    - ูุงุทุน
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - meter_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช
    # - screen_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุดุงุดุงุช
    # - seal_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุฃุฎุชุงู
    # - breaker_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูููุงุทุน
    # - purchase_order_id: ุฑูู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุดุฑุงุก
    
    meter_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='STS-METER').first()
    screen_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='STS-CIU-001').first()
    seal_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='SEAL-001').first()
    breaker_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='BREAKER-63A').first()
    
    created_units = {
        'meters': [],
        'screens': [],
        'seals': [],
        'breakers': []
    }
    
    total_amount = 0
    
    # ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช
    for serial in data['meter_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit(
            unit_code=f"STS-METER-{serial}",
            item_id=meter_item.id,
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock',
            location='Main Warehouse',
            received_date=datetime.now()
        )
        db.session.add(unit)
        created_units['meters'].append(unit)
        total_amount += meter_item.unit_price
    
    # ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุงูุดุงุดุงุช
    for serial in data['screen_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit(
            unit_code=f"STS-CIU-{serial}",
            item_id=screen_item.id,
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock',
            location='Main Warehouse',
            received_date=datetime.now()
        )
        db.session.add(unit)
        created_units['screens'].append(unit)
        total_amount += screen_item.unit_price
    
    # ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุงูุฃุฎุชุงู ูุงูููุงุทุน (ููุณ ุงูุทุฑููุฉ)
    for serial in data['seal_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit(
            unit_code=f"SEAL-{serial}",
            item_id=seal_item.id,
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock',
            location='Main Warehouse',
            received_date=datetime.now()
        )
        db.session.add(unit)
        created_units['seals'].append(unit)
        total_amount += seal_item.unit_price
    
    for serial in data['breaker_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit(
            unit_code=f"BREAKER-{serial}",
            item_id=breaker_item.id,
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock',
            location='Main Warehouse',
            received_date=datetime.now()
        )
        db.session.add(unit)
        created_units['breakers'].append(unit)
        total_amount += breaker_item.unit_price
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจู ุดุงูู
    journal_entry = JournalEntry(
        entry_date=datetime.now(),
        description=f"ุงุณุชูุจุงู ุญุฒูุฉ STS: {len(data['meter_serials'])} ุนุฏุงุฏ + ุดุงุดุงุช + ุฃุฎุชุงู + ููุงุทุน",
        debit_account='Inventory',
        debit_amount=total_amount,
        credit_account='Accounts Payable',
        credit_amount=total_amount,
        reference_id=data.get('purchase_order_id'),
        reference_type='purchase_order'
    )
    db.session.add(journal_entry)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'units_received': {
            'meters': len(created_units['meters']),
            'screens': len(created_units['screens']),
            'seals': len(created_units['seals']),
            'breakers': len(created_units['breakers'])
        },
        'total_amount': total_amount
    }, 201
```

### ุชุญุฏูุซ 7.3: ุทูุจ ูุตุฑู ุงูููุงุฏ (ูุญุฏูุซ)

**ุนูุฏ ุทูุจ ููุงุฏ ูุชุฑููุจ STS:**

```python
@app.route('/api/inventory/material-request-sts', methods=['POST'])
def create_sts_material_request():
    """
    ุฅูุดุงุก ุทูุจ ููุงุฏ ูุชุฑููุจ ุนุฏุงุฏ STS
    ูุชุถูู: ุนุฏุงุฏ + ุดุงุดุฉ + ุฎุชู + ูุงุทุน
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - station_id: ุงููุญุทุฉ
    # - subscription_type: 'sts' (ูุชุญุฏูุฏ ุงูููููุงุช ุชููุงุฆูุงู)
    # - quantity: ุนุฏุฏ ุงูุญุฒู ุงููุทููุจุฉ
    
    station = Station.query.get(data['station_id'])
    quantity = data['quantity']
    
    material_request = MaterialRequest(
        request_number=generate_mr_number(),
        station_id=station.id,
        request_type='sts_installation',
        status='pending',
        requested_date=datetime.now(),
        requested_by=current_user.username
    )
    
    # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุชูุงุตูู ุงูุทูุจ
    for i in range(quantity):
        # ุนุฏุงุฏ STS
        meter_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            item_id=InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='STS-METER').first().id,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        
        # ุดุงุดุฉ STS
        screen_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            item_id=InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='STS-CIU-001').first().id,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        
        # ุฎุชู
        seal_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            item_id=InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='SEAL-001').first().id,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        
        # ูุงุทุน
        breaker_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            item_id=InventoryItem.query.filter_by(item_code='BREAKER-63A').first().id,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        
        if not all([meter_unit, screen_unit, seal_unit, breaker_unit]):
            return {'error': 'ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ููููุงุช ูุงููุฉ ูู ุงููุฎุฒูู'}, 400
        
        # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุงูููููุงุช ููุทูุจ
        for unit in [meter_unit, screen_unit, seal_unit, breaker_unit]:
            request_line = MaterialRequestLine(
                material_request_id=material_request.id,
                inventory_unit_id=unit.id,
                item_id=unit.item_id,
                serial_number=unit.serial_number
            )
            db.session.add(request_line)
    
    db.session.add(material_request)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'request_id': material_request.id,
        'request_number': material_request.request_number,
        'components': {
            'meters': quantity,
            'screens': quantity,
            'seals': quantity,
            'breakers': quantity
        }
    }, 201

# API ูุตุฑู ุงูููุงุฏ
@app.route('/api/inventory/issue-sts-materials', methods=['POST'])
def issue_sts_materials():
    """
    ุตุฑู ููุงุฏ STS ูู ุงููุฎุฒู
    ูุชู ูุณุญ ุงูุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุชุณูุตููุฉ ูุฌููุน ุงูููููุงุช
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - material_request_id: ุทูุจ ุงูููุงุฏ
    # - meter_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงููุตุฑููุฉ
    # - screen_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุดุงุดุงุช ุงููุตุฑููุฉ
    # - seal_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูุฃุฎุชุงู ุงููุตุฑููุฉ
    # - breaker_serials: ุฃุฑูุงู ุงูููุงุทุน ุงููุตุฑููุฉ
    # - station_id: ุงููุญุทุฉ ุงููุณุชูุจูุฉ
    
    material_request = MaterialRequest.query.get(data['material_request_id'])
    station = Station.query.get(data['station_id'])
    
    issued_units = {
        'meters': [],
        'screens': [],
        'seals': [],
        'breakers': []
    }
    
    # ุตุฑู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช
    for serial in data['meter_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        if unit:
            unit.status = 'issued'
            unit.assigned_to = station.name
            unit.location = f"Station: {station.name}"
            unit.issued_date = datetime.now()
            issued_units['meters'].append(serial)
    
    # ุตุฑู ุงูุดุงุดุงุช
    for serial in data['screen_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        if unit:
            unit.status = 'issued'
            unit.assigned_to = station.name
            unit.location = f"Station: {station.name}"
            unit.issued_date = datetime.now()
            issued_units['screens'].append(serial)
    
    # ุตุฑู ุงูุฃุฎุชุงู ูุงูููุงุทุน (ููุณ ุงูุทุฑููุฉ)
    for serial in data['seal_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        if unit:
            unit.status = 'issued'
            unit.assigned_to = station.name
            unit.issued_date = datetime.now()
            issued_units['seals'].append(serial)
    
    for serial in data['breaker_serials']:
        unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
            serial_number=serial,
            status='in_stock'
        ).first()
        if unit:
            unit.status = 'issued'
            unit.assigned_to = station.name
            unit.issued_date = datetime.now()
            issued_units['breakers'].append(serial)
    
    material_request.status = 'issued'
    material_request.issued_date = datetime.now()
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'units_issued': issued_units,
        'assigned_to': station.name
    }, 200
```

### ุชุญุฏูุซ 8.3: ุชุทุจูู ุงูููู ุงูููุฏุงูู (ูุญุฏูุซ)

**ุนูุฏ ุชุฑููุจ ุนุฏุงุฏ STS:**

```python
@app.route('/api/installation/<installation_id>/complete-sts', methods=['POST'])
def complete_sts_installation(installation_id):
    """
    ุฅููุงู ุชุฑููุจ ุนุฏุงุฏ STS ูุน ุชุณููู ุงูุดุงุดุฉ ููุนููู
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    installation = Installation.query.get(installation_id)
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - meter_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ููุนุฏุงุฏ
    # - screen_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ููุดุงุดุฉ
    # - seal_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ููุฎุชู
    # - breaker_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ูููุงุทุน
    # - screen_delivered: ูู ุชู ุชุณููู ุงูุดุงุดุฉ ููุนูููุ
    # - customer_signature: ุชูููุน ุงูุนููู ุนูู ุงุณุชูุงู ุงูุดุงุดุฉ
    
    # ุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุงูููููุงุช
    meter_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['meter_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    screen_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['screen_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    seal_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['seal_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    breaker_unit = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['breaker_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    if not all([meter_unit, screen_unit, seal_unit, breaker_unit]):
        return {'error': 'ุฃุญุฏ ุงูููููุงุช ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏ'}, 400
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุฌููุน ุงูููููุงุช ุฅูู "ูุฑูุจ"
    for unit in [meter_unit, screen_unit, seal_unit, breaker_unit]:
        unit.status = 'installed'
        unit.installed_at_subscriber_id = installation.subscriber_id
        unit.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุชุฑููุจ
    installation.status = 'completed'
    installation.completion_date = datetime.now()
    installation.meter_serial = data['meter_serial']
    installation.screen_serial = data['screen_serial']
    installation.seal_serial = data['seal_serial']
    installation.breaker_serial = data['breaker_serial']
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุชุณููู ุงูุดุงุดุฉ
    if data.get('screen_delivered'):
        screen_delivery = ScreenDelivery(
            installation_id=installation.id,
            screen_serial=data['screen_serial'],
            delivery_date=datetime.now(),
            customer_signature=data.get('customer_signature'),
            technician_id=data['technician_id'],
            notes=data.get('notes')
        )
        db.session.add(screen_delivery)
    
    # ุญูุธ ุงูุตูุฑ
    if 'photos' in data:
        for photo_data in data['photos']:
            photo = InstallationPhoto(
                installation_id=installation.id,
                photo_url=save_photo(photo_data),
                photo_type=photo_data.get('type')  # 'meter', 'screen', 'installation'
            )
            db.session.add(photo)
    
    # ุชูุนูู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ูู ูุธุงู ุงูููุชุฑุฉ
    meter = installation.meter
    meter.is_active = True
    meter.activation_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุชูุนูู ุงูุดุงุดุฉ ููุนููู
    screen_activation = ScreenActivation(
        screen_serial=data['screen_serial'],
        subscriber_id=installation.subscriber_id,
        activation_date=datetime.now(),
        meter_serial=data['meter_serial']
    )
    db.session.add(screen_activation)
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'installation_id': installation.id,
        'meter_activated': True,
        'screen_delivered': data.get('screen_delivered'),
        'completion_date': installation.completion_date.isoformat()
    }, 200
```

---

### ุชุญุฏูุซ 9.2: ุงูุตูุงูุฉ ูุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู (ูุญุฏูุซ)

**ุนูุฏ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุดุงุดุฉ STS:**

```python
@app.route('/api/maintenance/work-orders/<wo_id>/replace-sts-screen', methods=['POST'])
def replace_sts_screen(wo_id):
    """
    ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุดุงุดุฉ STS ุชุงููุฉ
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(wo_id)
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - old_screen_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ููุดุงุดุฉ ุงูุชุงููุฉ
    # - new_screen_serial: ุงูุฑูู ุงูุชุณูุตูู ููุดุงุดุฉ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
    # - reason: ุณุจุจ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
    # - technician_id: ุงูููู
    
    # ุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุงูุดุงุดุงุช
    old_screen = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['old_screen_serial'],
        installed_at_subscriber_id=work_order.subscriber_id
    ).first()
    
    new_screen = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=data['new_screen_serial'],
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    if not old_screen or not new_screen:
        return {'error': 'ุฃุญุฏ ุงูุดุงุดุงุช ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏุฉ'}, 400
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุดุงุดุฉ ุงููุฏููุฉ
    old_screen.status = 'defective'
    old_screen.installed_at_subscriber_id = None
    old_screen.installation_date = None
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุดุงุดุฉ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
    new_screen.status = 'installed'
    new_screen.installed_at_subscriber_id = work_order.subscriber_id
    new_screen.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุนูููุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
    replacement_log = ComponentReplacement(
        work_order_id=work_order.id,
        component_type='sts_screen',
        old_unit_id=old_screen.id,
        new_unit_id=new_screen.id,
        reason=data['reason'],
        technician_id=data['technician_id'],
        replacement_date=datetime.now()
    )
    db.session.add(replacement_log)
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ููู ุงููุดุชุฑู
    subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(work_order.subscriber_id)
    subscriber.screen_serial = data['new_screen_serial']
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุชุณููู ุงูุดุงุดุฉ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
    screen_delivery = ScreenDelivery(
        work_order_id=work_order.id,
        screen_serial=data['new_screen_serial'],
        delivery_date=datetime.now(),
        technician_id=data['technician_id'],
        notes=f"ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุดุงุดุฉ ุชุงููุฉ: {data['old_screen_serial']}"
    )
    db.session.add(screen_delivery)
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'replacement_id': replacement_log.id,
        'old_screen': data['old_screen_serial'],
        'new_screen': data['new_screen_serial'],
        'replacement_date': replacement_log.replacement_date.isoformat()
    }, 200
```

| ููุน ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ | ููุน ุงูุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู | ูุจูุบ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู | ูุจูุบ ุงูุชุฃููู | ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู |
|-----------|--------------|-------------|-----------|---------|

| **STS** | ููุฒูู | 7,000 | **0** | 7,000 |

| **IoT** | ุชุฌุงุฑู | 15,000 | 45,000 | 60,000 |

### ุงููุดููุฉ ุงูุณุงุจูุฉ:
- โ ููุณ ุงูููุทู ุงููุงูู ูุฌููุน ุงูุฃููุงุน

- โ ุฃุฎุทุงุก ูุฏููุฉ ูุชูุฑุฑุฉ
