## ๐ ุงูููุงู ุงููุฑุนูุฉ:

### 8.2.1: ุจูุงุก ุฌุฏูู ูุญุฑู ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ (Pricing Engine Table)

**ุงููุตู:** ุฌุฏูู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุจูุงูุงุช ูุฑู ูุชุฎุฒูู ููุงุนุฏ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ.

```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
class PricingRule(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    rule_code = db.Column(db.String(50), unique=True)
    meter_type = db.Column(db.String(50))  # 'traditional', 'sts', 'iot'
    usage_type = db.Column(db.String(50))  # 'residential', 'commercial'
    subscription_fee = db.Column(db.Float)  # ุฑุณู ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู
    deposit_amount = db.Column(db.Float)  # ูุจูุบ ุงูุชุฃููู
    deposit_required = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=True)  # ูู ุงูุชุฃููู ูุทููุจุ
    activation_fee = db.Column(db.Float, default=0)  # ุฑุณู ุงูุชูุนูู
    installation_fee = db.Column(db.Float, default=0)  # ุฑุณู ุงูุชุฑููุจ
    description = db.Column(db.String(200))
    is_active = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=True)
    created_date = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_date = db.Column(db.DateTime, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)
    created_by = db.Column(db.String(100))
    updated_by = db.Column(db.String(100))
    
    def calculate_total(self):
        """ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุจูุบ ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู"""
        total = self.subscription_fee
        if self.deposit_required:
            total += self.deposit_amount
        total += self.activation_fee
        total += self.installation_fee
        return total

# ูุซุงู ุนูู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุฃูููุฉ
pricing_rules = [
    PricingRule(
        rule_code='TRAD-RES',
        meter_type='traditional',
        usage_type='residential',
        subscription_fee=5000,
        deposit_amount=35000,
        deposit_required=True,
        activation_fee=500,
        installation_fee=1000,
        description='ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชูููุฏู - ููุฒูู'
    ),
    PricingRule(
        rule_code='TRAD-COM',
        meter_type='traditional',
        usage_type='commercial',
        subscription_fee=10000,
        deposit_amount=50000,
        deposit_required=True,
        activation_fee=1000,
        installation_fee=2000,
        description='ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชูููุฏู - ุชุฌุงุฑู'
    ),
    PricingRule(
        rule_code='STS-RES',
        meter_type='sts',
        usage_type='residential',
        subscription_fee=7000,
        deposit_amount=0,
        deposit_required=False,  # โญ ูุง ููุฌุฏ ุชุฃููู
        activation_fee=500,
        installation_fee=1000,
        description='ุนุฏุงุฏ STS - ููุฒูู'
    ),
    PricingRule(
        rule_code='STS-COM',
        meter_type='sts',
        usage_type='commercial',
        subscription_fee=12000,
        deposit_amount=0,
        deposit_required=False,  # โญ ูุง ููุฌุฏ ุชุฃููู
        activation_fee=1000,
        installation_fee=2000,
        description='ุนุฏุงุฏ STS - ุชุฌุงุฑู'
    ),
    PricingRule(
        rule_code='IOT-RES',
        meter_type='iot',
        usage_type='residential',
        subscription_fee=6000,
        deposit_amount=30000,
        deposit_required=True,
        activation_fee=500,
        installation_fee=1500,
        description='ุนุฏุงุฏ IoT - ููุฒูู'
    ),
]
```

### 8.2.2: ูุงุฌูุฉ ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ููุงุนุฏ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ (Pricing Rules Management)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุงุฌูุฉ ููุฏูุฑ ุงููุธุงู ูุชุนุฏูู ููุงุนุณ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 8.2.2.1: ุนุฑุถ ุฌููุน ููุงุนุณ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ
- 8.2.2.2: ุฅุถุงูุฉ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
- 8.2.2.3: ุชุนุฏูู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ููุฌูุฏุฉ
- 8.2.2.4: ุชูุนูู/ุชุนุทูู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ
- 8.2.2.5: ุนุฑุถ ุงูุณุฌู ุงูุชุงุฑูุฎู ููุชุบููุฑุงุช

**ุงูููุฏ ุงููููุฐุฌู:**
```python
# API ูุฌูุจ ููุงุนุณ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ
@app.route('/api/pricing/rules', methods=['GET'])
@admin_required
def get_pricing_rules():
    """ุฌูุจ ุฌููุน ููุงุนุณ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ"""
    
    rules = PricingRule.query.filter_by(is_active=True).all()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'rules': [
            {
                'id': rule.id,
                'rule_code': rule.rule_code,
                'meter_type': rule.meter_type,
                'usage_type': rule.usage_type,
                'subscription_fee': rule.subscription_fee,
                'deposit_amount': rule.deposit_amount,
                'deposit_required': rule.deposit_required,
                'total': rule.calculate_total(),
                'description': rule.description
            }
            for rule in rules
        ]
    }, 200

# API ูุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
@app.route('/api/pricing/rules', methods=['POST'])
@admin_required
def create_pricing_rule():
    """ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ"""
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุนุฏู ูุฌูุฏ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ูุดุงุจูุฉ
    existing_rule = PricingRule.query.filter_by(
        meter_type=data['meter_type'],
        usage_type=data['usage_type']
    ).first()
    
    if existing_rule:
        return {'error': 'ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ูุดุงุจูุฉ ููุฌูุฏุฉ ุจุงููุนู'}, 400
    
    rule = PricingRule(
        rule_code=data['rule_code'],
        meter_type=data['meter_type'],
        usage_type=data['usage_type'],
        subscription_fee=data['subscription_fee'],
        deposit_amount=data.get('deposit_amount', 0),
        deposit_required=data.get('deposit_required', True),
        activation_fee=data.get('activation_fee', 0),
        installation_fee=data.get('installation_fee', 0),
        description=data.get('description'),
        created_by=current_user.username
    )
    
    db.session.add(rule)
    db.session.commit()
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ูู ุงูุณุฌู ุงูุชุงุฑูุฎู
    audit_log = AuditLog(
        action='create_pricing_rule',
        resource_type='PricingRule',
        resource_id=rule.id,
        details=f"ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ: {rule.rule_code}",
        user_id=current_user.id
    )
    db.session.add(audit_log)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'rule_id': rule.id,
        'rule_code': rule.rule_code,
        'total': rule.calculate_total()
    }, 201

# API ูุชุญุฏูุซ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ
@app.route('/api/pricing/rules/<rule_id>', methods=['PUT'])
@admin_required
def update_pricing_rule(rule_id):
    """ุชุญุฏูุซ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ููุฌูุฏุฉ"""
    
    rule = PricingRule.query.get(rule_id)
    if not rule:
        return {'error': 'ุงููุงุนุฏุฉ ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏุฉ'}, 404
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุชุบููุฑุงุช
    changes = {}
    
    if 'subscription_fee' in data and data['subscription_fee'] != rule.subscription_fee:
        changes['subscription_fee'] = f"{rule.subscription_fee} โ {data['subscription_fee']}"
        rule.subscription_fee = data['subscription_fee']
    
    if 'deposit_amount' in data and data['deposit_amount'] != rule.deposit_amount:
        changes['deposit_amount'] = f"{rule.deposit_amount} โ {data['deposit_amount']}"
        rule.deposit_amount = data['deposit_amount']
    
    if 'deposit_required' in data and data['deposit_required'] != rule.deposit_required:
        changes['deposit_required'] = f"{rule.deposit_required} โ {data['deposit_required']}"
        rule.deposit_required = data['deposit_required']
    
    if 'activation_fee' in data:
        changes['activation_fee'] = f"{rule.activation_fee} โ {data['activation_fee']}"
        rule.activation_fee = data['activation_fee']
    
    if 'installation_fee' in data:
        changes['installation_fee'] = f"{rule.installation_fee} โ {data['installation_fee']}"
        rule.installation_fee = data['installation_fee']
    
    rule.updated_by = current_user.username
    rule.updated_date = datetime.now()
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุชุบููุฑุงุช
    audit_log = AuditLog(
        action='update_pricing_rule',
        resource_type='PricingRule',
        resource_id=rule.id,
        details=f"ุชุญุฏูุซ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ: {rule.rule_code}. ุงูุชุบููุฑุงุช: {changes}",
        user_id=current_user.id
    )
    db.session.add(audit_log)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'rule_id': rule.id,
        'changes': changes,
        'new_total': rule.calculate_total()
    }, 200
```

---

### 8.2.3: ูุญุฑู ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูุงููู (Cost Calculation Engine)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุญุฑู ูุญุณุจ ุงูุชูุงููู ุชููุงุฆูุงู ุจูุงุกู ุนูู ููุน ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ูุงูุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู.

```python
class SubscriptionCostCalculator:
    """ูุญุฑู ุญุณุงุจ ุชูุงููู ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู"""
    
    @staticmethod
    def get_pricing_rule(meter_type, usage_type):
        """ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ ุงูููุงุณุจุฉ"""
        
        rule = PricingRule.query.filter_by(
            meter_type=meter_type,
            usage_type=usage_type,
            is_active=True
        ).first()
        
        if not rule:
            raise ValueError(f"ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุชุณุนูุฑ ูู {meter_type} - {usage_type}")
        
        return rule
    
    @staticmethod
    def calculate_subscription_cost(meter_type, usage_type):
        """ุญุณุงุจ ุชูููุฉ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู ุงููุงููุฉ"""
        
        rule = SubscriptionCostCalculator.get_pricing_rule(meter_type, usage_type)
        
        return {
            'subscription_fee': rule.subscription_fee,
            'deposit_amount': rule.deposit_amount if rule.deposit_required else 0,
            'deposit_required': rule.deposit_required,
            'activation_fee': rule.activation_fee,
            'installation_fee': rule.installation_fee,
            'total': rule.calculate_total(),
            'rule_code': rule.rule_code,
            'description': rule.description
        }
    
    @staticmethod
    def calculate_invoice_items(meter_type, usage_type):
        """ุญุณุงุจ ุจููุฏ ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ"""
        
        rule = SubscriptionCostCalculator.get_pricing_rule(meter_type, usage_type)
        
        invoice_items = [
            {
                'item_type': 'subscription_fee',
                'description': f'ุฑุณู ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู - {rule.description}',
                'amount': rule.subscription_fee
            },
            {
                'item_type': 'activation_fee',
                'description': 'ุฑุณู ุงูุชูุนูู',
                'amount': rule.activation_fee
            },
            {
                'item_type': 'installation_fee',
                'description': 'ุฑุณู ุงูุชุฑููุจ',
                'amount': rule.installation_fee
            }
        ]
        
        # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุงูุชุฃููู ููุท ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ูุทููุจุงู
        if rule.deposit_required:
            invoice_items.append({
                'item_type': 'deposit',
                'description': 'ูุจูุบ ุงูุชุฃููู',
                'amount': rule.deposit_amount
            })
        
        return invoice_items
```

### 8.2.4: ุชุญุฏูุซ ูููุฐุฌ ุทูุจ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู (Updated Subscription Request)

**ุงููุตู:** ุชุญุฏูุซ ูููุฐุฌ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู ููุณุชุฎุฏู ูุญุฑู ุงูุชุณุนูุฑ.

```python
@app.route('/api/subscriptions/new-subscription', methods=['POST'])
def create_new_subscription():
    """
    ุฅูุดุงุก ุงุดุชุฑุงู ุฌุฏูุฏ ูุน ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูุงููู ุชููุงุฆูุงู
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - subscriber_name
    # - subscriber_phone
    # - subscriber_address
    # - meter_type: 'traditional', 'sts', 'iot'
    # - usage_type: 'residential', 'commercial'
    # - station_id
    
    try:
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูุงููู ุชููุงุฆูุงู
        cost_breakdown = SubscriptionCostCalculator.calculate_subscription_cost(
            meter_type=data['meter_type'],
            usage_type=data['usage_type']
        )
        
        invoice_items = SubscriptionCostCalculator.calculate_invoice_items(
            meter_type=data['meter_type'],
            usage_type=data['usage_type']
        )
        
    except ValueError as e:
        return {'error': str(e)}, 400
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุดุชุฑู
    subscriber = Subscriber(
        name=data['subscriber_name'],
        phone=data['subscriber_phone'],
        address=data['subscriber_address'],
        meter_type=data['meter_type'],
        usage_type=data['usage_type'],
        station_id=data['station_id'],
        status='pending',
        created_date=datetime.now()
    )
    
    db.session.add(subscriber)
    db.session.flush()  # ููุญุตูู ุนูู subscriber_id
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
    invoice = Invoice(
        subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
        invoice_type='subscription',
        invoice_number=generate_invoice_number(),
        issue_date=datetime.now(),
        due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15),
        status='unpaid',
        total_amount=cost_breakdown['total'],
        notes=f"ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุดุชุฑุงู - {cost_breakdown['description']}"
    )
    
    db.session.add(invoice)
    db.session.flush()
    
    # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุจููุฏ ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
    for item in invoice_items:
        invoice_line = InvoiceLineItem(
            invoice_id=invoice.id,
            item_type=item['item_type'],
            description=item['description'],
            amount=item['amount'],
            quantity=1
        )
        db.session.add(invoice_line)
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจู
    journal_entry = JournalEntry(
        entry_date=datetime.now(),
        description=f"ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุดุชุฑุงู ุฌุฏูุฏ - {subscriber.name}",
        debit_account='Accounts Receivable',
        debit_amount=cost_breakdown['total'],
        credit_account='Service Revenue',
        credit_amount=cost_breakdown['subscription_fee'],
        reference_id=invoice.id,
        reference_type='invoice'
    )
    
    # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ููุฏ ูููุตู ููุชุฃููู ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ููุฌูุฏุงู
    if cost_breakdown['deposit_required'] and cost_breakdown['deposit_amount'] > 0:
        deposit_entry = JournalEntry(
            entry_date=datetime.now(),
            description=f"ุงุณุชูุจุงู ูุจูุบ ุชุฃููู - {subscriber.name}",
            debit_account='Cash',
            debit_amount=cost_breakdown['deposit_amount'],
            credit_account='Customer Deposits',
            credit_amount=cost_breakdown['deposit_amount'],
            reference_id=invoice.id,
            reference_type='invoice'
        )
        db.session.add(deposit_entry)
    
    db.session.add(journal_entry)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'subscriber_id': subscriber.id,
        'invoice_id': invoice.id,
        'invoice_number': invoice.invoice_number,
        'cost_breakdown': {
            'subscription_fee': cost_breakdown['subscription_fee'],
            'deposit_amount': cost_breakdown['deposit_amount'],
            'deposit_required': cost_breakdown['deposit_required'],
            'activation_fee': cost_breakdown['activation_fee'],
            'installation_fee': cost_breakdown['installation_fee'],
            'total': cost_breakdown['total']
        },
        'invoice_items': invoice_items
    }, 201
```

### 8.2.5: ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุชุณุฌูู ุงููุญุฏุซุฉ (Updated Registration Interface)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุชุณุฌูู ุชุนุฑุถ ุงูุชูุงููู ุชููุงุฆูุงู.

**ุงูููุงู:**
- 8.2.5.1: ุนูุฏ ุงุฎุชูุงุฑ "ููุน ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ" ู "ููุน ุงูุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู"ุ ูุนุฑุถ ุงููุธุงู ุงูุชูุงููู ุชููุงุฆูุงู
- 8.2.5.2: ุฅุฎูุงุก ุญููู ุงูุชุฃููู ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ููุน ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ STS
- 8.2.5.3: ุนุฑุถ ุชูุตูู ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ ูุจู ุงูุญูุธ
- 8.2.5.4: ุชุฃููุฏ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ูุจู ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ

**ุงูุดุงุดุฉ:**

# ุชุญุฏูุซ ูุชูุฏู: ุณููุงุฑูููุงุช ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูุงูุชุฑููุฉ ุงููุนูุฏุฉ
## Advanced Update: Complex Replacement & Upgrade Scenarios

**ุงูุฃููููุฉ:** ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู  
**ุงูุชุฃุซูุฑ:** ุงูููุงู 7ุ 9ุ 10  
**ุงูุญุงูุฉ:** ุชุญุฏูุซ ุดุงูู

## ๐ฏ ุงููุฏู:

ุจูุงุก ูุนุงูุฌุงุช ุฐููุฉ ููุนูููุงุช ุงููุนูุฏุฉ: ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุชุงููุ ุชุฑููุฉ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงูุ ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุณุชุนููุฉ.

## ๐ ุงูุณููุงุฑูููุงุช ุงูุซูุงุซุฉ:

### ุงูุณููุงุฑูู 1๏ธโฃ: ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุนุฏุงุฏ ุนุงุฏู ุชุงูู

**ุงูุญุงูุฉ:** ุนููู ูุฏูู ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชูููุฏู ุชุนุทู

**ุงููุดููุฉ ุงูุญุงููุฉ:**
- โ ุญุณุงุจ ูุฏูู ููุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููููุฏ
- โ ูุฑุงุฑ ูุฏูู ุญูู ุชูููุฉ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ
- โ ุฃุฎุทุงุก ูู ุงูููุชุฑุฉ

**ุงูุญู ุงูููุชุฑุญ:**

#### 10.4: ูุนุงูุฌ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุชุงูู (Defective Meter Replacement Wizard)

```python
class DefectiveMeterReplacementWizard:
    """ูุนุงูุฌ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุชุงูู"""
    
    def __init__(self, work_order_id, subscriber_id):
        self.work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(work_order_id)
        self.subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(subscriber_id)
        self.steps = []
    
    def step_1_estimate_consumption(self):
        """ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 1: ุชูุฏูุฑ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููููุฏ"""
        
        # ุฌูุจ ุขุฎุฑ 3 ููุงุชูุฑ
        recent_invoices = Invoice.query.filter_by(
            subscriber_id=self.subscriber.id,
            invoice_type='consumption'
        ).order_by(Invoice.issue_date.desc()).limit(3).all()
        
        if len(recent_invoices) < 3:
            return {
                'status': 'warning',
                'message': 'ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ููุงุชูุฑ ูุงููุฉ ูุญุณุงุจ ุงููุชูุณุท'
            }
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ูุชูุณุท ุงูุงุณุชููุงู
        total_consumption = sum([inv.consumption_kwh for inv in recent_invoices])
        average_consumption = total_consumption / len(recent_invoices)
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุชุฑุฉ ุงูููููุฏุฉ
        last_reading_date = recent_invoices[0].issue_date
        missing_days = (datetime.now() - last_reading_date).days
        missing_months = missing_days / 30
        
        # ุชูุฏูุฑ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููููุฏ
        estimated_consumption = average_consumption * missing_months
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูููุฉ
        estimated_cost = estimated_consumption * 1.5  # ุณุนุฑ ุชูุฑูุจู
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'average_consumption': average_consumption,
            'missing_days': missing_days,
            'missing_months': round(missing_months, 2),
            'estimated_consumption': round(estimated_consumption, 2),
            'estimated_cost': round(estimated_cost, 2),
            'last_reading_date': last_reading_date.isoformat()
        }
    
    def step_2_determine_replacement_cost(self):
        """ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 2: ุชุญุฏูุฏ ุชูููุฉ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ"""
        
        # ุฌูุจ ุณุนุฑ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ูู ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงูุฃุณุนุงุฑ
        meter_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(
            item_code='TRADITIONAL-METER'
        ).first()
        
        meter_cost = meter_item.unit_price if meter_item else 2000
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'meter_cost': meter_cost,
            'options': [
                {
                    'option': 'full_charge',
                    'description': 'ุชุญููู ุงูุชูููุฉ ูุงููุฉ ุนูู ุงูุนููู',
                    'amount': meter_cost
                },
                {
                    'option': 'half_charge',
                    'description': 'ุชุญููู 50% ูู ุงูุชูููุฉ',
                    'amount': meter_cost / 2
                },
                {
                    'option': 'free_replacement',
                    'description': 'ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูุฌุงูู (ุถูุงู)',
                    'amount': 0
                }
            ]
        }
    
    def step_3_create_invoices(self, consumption_cost, replacement_option):
        """ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 3: ุฅูุดุงุก ุงูููุงุชูุฑ"""
        
        invoices = []
        
        # ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููููุฏ
        consumption_invoice = Invoice(
            subscriber_id=self.subscriber.id,
            invoice_type='consumption',
            invoice_number=generate_invoice_number(),
            issue_date=datetime.now(),
            due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15),
            status='unpaid',
            total_amount=consumption_cost,
            notes='ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุณุชููุงู ููููุฏ - ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชุงูู'
        )
        db.session.add(consumption_invoice)
        invoices.append(consumption_invoice)
        
        # ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุชูููุฉ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ (ุฅุฐุง ูู ุชูู ูุฌุงููุฉ)
        if replacement_option != 'free_replacement':
            meter_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(
                item_code='TRADITIONAL-METER'
            ).first()
            
            if replacement_option == 'full_charge':
                meter_charge = meter_item.unit_price
            elif replacement_option == 'half_charge':
                meter_charge = meter_item.unit_price / 2
            
            meter_invoice = Invoice(
                subscriber_id=self.subscriber.id,
                invoice_type='replacement',
                invoice_number=generate_invoice_number(),
                issue_date=datetime.now(),
                due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15),
                status='unpaid',
                total_amount=meter_charge,
                notes=f'ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุนุฏุงุฏ - {replacement_option}'
            )
            db.session.add(meter_invoice)
            invoices.append(meter_invoice)
        
        db.session.commit()
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'invoices_created': len(invoices),
            'total_amount': sum([inv.total_amount for inv in invoices])
        }
    
    def execute(self, replacement_option):
        """ุชูููุฐ ุงููุนุงูุฌ ุงููุงูู"""
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 1
        consumption_estimate = self.step_1_estimate_consumption()
        if consumption_estimate['status'] != 'success':
            return consumption_estimate
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 2
        replacement_cost = self.step_2_determine_replacement_cost()
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 3
        invoices = self.step_3_create_invoices(
            consumption_estimate['estimated_cost'],
            replacement_option
        )
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'consumption_estimate': consumption_estimate,
            'replacement_cost': replacement_cost,
            'invoices': invoices
        }

# API ูุชูููุฐ ูุนุงูุฌ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู
@app.route('/api/maintenance/defective-meter-replacement', methods=['POST'])
def execute_defective_meter_replacement():
    """ุชูููุฐ ูุนุงูุฌ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุชุงูู"""
    
    data = request.json
    
    wizard = DefectiveMeterReplacementWizard(
        work_order_id=data['work_order_id'],
        subscriber_id=data['subscriber_id']
    )
    
    result = wizard.execute(data['replacement_option'])
    
    return result, 200
```

---

### ุงูุณููุงุฑูู 2๏ธโฃ: ุชุฑููุฉ ุนุฏุงุฏ ุนุงุฏู ุฅูู STS

**ุงูุญุงูุฉ:** ุนููู ูุฑูุฏ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ ูู ุชูููุฏู ุฅูู ุฏูุน ูุณุจู

**ุงููุดููุฉ ุงูุญุงููุฉ:**
- โ ุญุณุงุจ ูุฏูู ูุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ
- โ ุฅูุบุงุก ูุฏูู ููุชุฃููู
- โ ุฃุฎุทุงุก ูู ุชุญุฏูุฏ ุงูุฃูููุฉ

**ุงูุญู ุงูููุชุฑุญ:**

#### 10.5: ูุนุงูุฌ ุชุฑููุฉ ููุน ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู (Subscription Upgrade Wizard)

```python
class SubscriptionUpgradeWizard:
    """ูุนุงูุฌ ุชุฑููุฉ ููุน ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู"""
    
    def __init__(self, subscriber_id):
        self.subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(subscriber_id)
    
    def check_eligibility(self):
        """ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุฃูููุฉ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ"""
        
        # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู
        last_payment_date = self.subscriber.last_payment_date
        days_since_last_payment = (datetime.now() - last_payment_date).days
        
        if days_since_last_payment > 180:  # ุฃูุซุฑ ูู 6 ุฃุดูุฑ
            status = 'inactive'
            upgrade_type = 'new_subscription'  # ุณุนุฑ ูุงูู ุฌุฏูุฏ
            upgrade_price = 35000  # ุณุนุฑ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู ุงููุงูู
        else:
            status = 'active'
            upgrade_type = 'upgrade'  # ุณุนุฑ ุชุฑููุฉ ูุฎูุถ
            upgrade_price = 20000  # ุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'subscriber_status': status,
            'upgrade_type': upgrade_type,
            'upgrade_price': upgrade_price,
            'last_payment_date': last_payment_date.isoformat(),
            'days_since_last_payment': days_since_last_payment
        }
    
    def cancel_deposit(self):
        """ุฅูุบุงุก ุงูุชุฃููู ุงููุฏูู"""
        
        # ุฌูุจ ุฑุตูุฏ ุงูุชุฃููู ุงูุญุงูู
        deposit_balance = self.subscriber.deposit_balance
        
        if deposit_balance > 0:
            # ุฅูุดุงุก ุณูุฏ ุฅูุบุงุก ุชุฃููู
            deposit_cancellation = DepositCancellation(
                subscriber_id=self.subscriber.id,
                cancellation_date=datetime.now(),
                cancelled_amount=deposit_balance,
                reason='ุชุฑููุฉ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู ูู ุชูููุฏู ุฅูู STS',
                status='pending'
            )
            db.session.add(deposit_cancellation)
            
            # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุฑุตูุฏ ุงูุชุฃููู
            self.subscriber.deposit_balance = 0
            
            db.session.commit()
            
            return {
                'status': 'success',
                'cancelled_amount': deposit_balance,
                'cancellation_id': deposit_cancellation.id
            }
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'cancelled_amount': 0,
            'message': 'ูุง ููุฌุฏ ุชุฃููู ูุฅูุบุงุคู'
        }
    
    def create_upgrade_invoice(self, upgrade_price, cancelled_deposit):
        """ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ"""
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุจูุบ ุงููุณุชุญู
        amount_due = upgrade_price - cancelled_deposit
        
        invoice = Invoice(
            subscriber_id=self.subscriber.id,
            invoice_type='upgrade',
            invoice_number=generate_invoice_number(),
            issue_date=datetime.now(),
            due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15),
            status='unpaid',
            total_amount=max(amount_due, 0),  # ูุง ูููู ุฃู ูููู ุณุงูุจุงู
            notes=f'ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุชุฑููุฉ - ูู ุชูููุฏู ุฅูู STS'
        )
        
        # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุจููุฏ ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
        invoice_line_1 = InvoiceLineItem(
            invoice_id=invoice.id,
            item_type='upgrade_fee',
            description='ุฑุณู ุงูุชุฑููุฉ ุฅูู STS',
            amount=upgrade_price,
            quantity=1
        )
        
        if cancelled_deposit > 0:
            invoice_line_2 = InvoiceLineItem(
                invoice_id=invoice.id,
                item_type='deposit_credit',
                description='ุฎุตู ุงูุชุฃููู ุงูููุบู',
                amount=-cancelled_deposit,
                quantity=1
            )
            db.session.add(invoice_line_2)
        
        db.session.add(invoice_line_1)
        db.session.add(invoice)
        db.session.commit()
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'invoice_id': invoice.id,
            'invoice_number': invoice.invoice_number,
            'amount_due': max(amount_due, 0)
        }
    
    def create_upgrade_work_order(self):
        """ุฅูุดุงุก ุฃูุฑ ุนูู ุงูุชุฑููุฉ"""
        
        # ุฃูุฑ ุนูู ุงูุชุฑููุฉ ูุชุถูู:
        # 1 ร ุนุฏุงุฏ STS
        # 1 ร ุดุงุดุฉ ุนุฑุถ STS
        # 1 ร ุฎุชู ุฌุฏูุฏ
        # 0 ร ูุงุทุน (ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงููุงุทุน ุงููุฏูู)
        
        work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder(
            work_order_number=generate_wo_number(),
            subscriber_id=self.subscriber.id,
            request_type='upgrade',
            reason='ุชุฑููุฉ ูู ุชูููุฏู ุฅูู STS',
            priority='normal',
            status='new'
        )
        
        db.session.add(work_order)
        db.session.commit()
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'work_order_id': work_order.id,
            'work_order_number': work_order.work_order_number,
            'components': {
                'sts_meter': 1,
                'sts_screen': 1,
                'seal': 1,
                'breaker': 0  # ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงููุฏูู
            }
        }
    
    def execute(self):
        """ุชูููุฐ ูุนุงูุฌ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ ุงููุงูู"""
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 1: ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุงูุฃูููุฉ
        eligibility = self.check_eligibility()
        if eligibility['status'] != 'success':
            return eligibility
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 2: ุฅูุบุงุก ุงูุชุฃููู
        deposit_cancellation = self.cancel_deposit()
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 3: ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ
        invoice = self.create_upgrade_invoice(
            eligibility['upgrade_price'],
            deposit_cancellation.get('cancelled_amount', 0)
        )
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 4: ุฅูุดุงุก ุฃูุฑ ุนูู ุงูุชุฑููุฉ
        work_order = self.create_upgrade_work_order()
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'eligibility': eligibility,
            'deposit_cancellation': deposit_cancellation,
            'invoice': invoice,
            'work_order': work_order
        }

# API ูุชูููุฐ ูุนุงูุฌ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ
@app.route('/api/subscriptions/upgrade-subscription', methods=['POST'])
def execute_subscription_upgrade():
    """ุชูููุฐ ูุนุงูุฌ ุชุฑููุฉ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู"""
    
    data = request.json
    
    wizard = SubscriptionUpgradeWizard(subscriber_id=data['subscriber_id'])
    result = wizard.execute()
    
    return result, 200
```

### ุงูุณููุงุฑูู 3๏ธโฃ: ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุณุชุนููุฉ ูุงูุชุงููุฉ

**ุงูุญุงูุฉ:** ุชุชุจุน ุงูุนุฏุงุฏุงุช ุงููุฑุชุฌุนุฉ ูุงูุชุงููุฉ

**ุงููุดููุฉ ุงูุญุงููุฉ:**
- โ ุนุฏู ูุถูุญ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุณุชุนููุฉ
- โ ุนุฏู ูุนุฑูุฉ ุฃูู ุชูุฌุฏ ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงูุชุงููุฉ
- โ ุตุนูุจุฉ ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงูุตุงูุญุฉ

**ุงูุญู ุงูููุชุฑุญ:**

#### 7.4: ูุณุชูุฏุนุงุช ุงูุชุฑุงุถูุฉ (Virtual Warehouses)

```python
# ูููุฐุฌ ุงููุณุชูุฏุน ุงูุงูุชุฑุงุถู
class VirtualWarehouse(db.Model):
    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)
    warehouse_code = db.Column(db.String(50), unique=True)
    warehouse_name = db.Column(db.String(100))
    warehouse_type = db.Column(db.String(50))  # 'main', 'station', 'virtual'
    location = db.Column(db.String(200))
    description = db.Column(db.Text)
    is_active = db.Column(db.Boolean, default=True)
    created_date = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)

# ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุณุชูุฏุนุงุช ุงูุงูุชุฑุงุถูุฉ
warehouses = [
    VirtualWarehouse(
        warehouse_code='MAIN-NEW',
        warehouse_name='ุงููุฎุฒู ุงูุฑุฆูุณู - ุฌุฏูุฏ',
        warehouse_type='main',
        location='Main Warehouse',
        description='ุฃุตูุงู ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ูู ุงูููุฑุฏูู'
    ),
    VirtualWarehouse(
        warehouse_code='STATION-NEW',
        warehouse_name='ูุฎุฒู ุงููุญุทุฉ - ุฌุฏูุฏ',
        warehouse_type='station',
        location='Power Station',
        description='ุฃุตูุงู ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ูู ุงููุญุทุฉ'
    ),
    VirtualWarehouse(
        warehouse_code='STATION-USED',
        warehouse_name='ูุฎุฒู ุงููุญุทุฉ - ูุณุชุนูู',
        warehouse_type='station',
        location='Power Station - Used Items',
        description='ุฃุตูุงู ูุณุชุนููุฉ ุตุงูุญุฉ ููุฅุนุงุฏุฉ'
    ),
    VirtualWarehouse(
        warehouse_code='STATION-DEFECTIVE',
        warehouse_name='ูุฎุฒู ุงููุญุทุฉ - ุชุงูู',
        warehouse_type='station',
        location='Power Station - Defective Items',
        description='ุฃุตูุงู ุชุงููุฉ ุจุงูุชุธุงุฑ ุงูุฅุตูุงุญ ุฃู ุงูุชุฎุฑูุฏ'
    ),
]

# ุชุญุฏูุซ ูููุฐุฌ ุงููุฎุฒูู
class InventoryUnit(db.Model):
    # ... ุงูุญููู ุงูููุฌูุฏุฉ ...
    warehouse_id = db.Column(db.Integer, db.ForeignKey('virtual_warehouse.id'))
    warehouse = db.relationship('VirtualWarehouse')
    item_condition = db.Column(db.String(50))  # 'new', 'used', 'defective'
    condition_notes = db.Column(db.Text)
    last_location_update = db.Column(db.DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)

# API ูููู ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุจูู ุงููุณุชูุฏุนุงุช
@app.route('/api/inventory/transfer-unit', methods=['POST'])
def transfer_inventory_unit():
    """ููู ุตูู ูู ูุณุชูุฏุน ุฅูู ุขุฎุฑ"""
    
    data = request.json
    
    unit = InventoryUnit.query.get(data['unit_id'])
    new_warehouse = VirtualWarehouse.query.get(data['warehouse_id'])
    
    if not unit or not new_warehouse:
        return {'error': 'ุงูุตูู ุฃู ุงููุณุชูุฏุน ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏ'}, 404
    
    # ุชุณุฌูู ุงูููู
    old_warehouse = unit.warehouse
    unit.warehouse_id = new_warehouse.id
    unit.item_condition = data.get('condition', unit.item_condition)
    unit.condition_notes = data.get('notes')
    unit.last_location_update = datetime.now()
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ุณุฌู ููู
    transfer_log = InventoryTransferLog(
        unit_id=unit.id,
        from_warehouse_id=old_warehouse.id,
        to_warehouse_id=new_warehouse.id,
        transfer_date=datetime.now(),
        reason=data.get('reason'),
        transferred_by=current_user.username
    )
    
    db.session.add(transfer_log)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'unit_id': unit.id,
        'from_warehouse': old_warehouse.warehouse_name,
        'to_warehouse': new_warehouse.warehouse_name,
        'condition': unit.item_condition
    }, 200

# API ูุนุฑุถ ุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช ุงููุณุชูุฏุนุงุช
@app.route('/api/inventory/warehouse-statistics', methods=['GET'])
def get_warehouse_statistics():
    """ุนุฑุถ ุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช ุงููุณุชูุฏุนุงุช"""
    
    warehouses = VirtualWarehouse.query.filter_by(is_active=True).all()
    
    statistics = []
    for warehouse in warehouses:
        units = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(warehouse_id=warehouse.id).all()
        
        statistics.append({
            'warehouse_id': warehouse.id,
            'warehouse_name': warehouse.warehouse_name,
            'total_units': len(units),
            'by_condition': {
                'new': len([u for u in units if u.item_condition == 'new']),
                'used': len([u for u in units if u.item_condition == 'used']),
                'defective': len([u for u in units if u.item_condition == 'defective'])
            },
            'by_type': {}
        })
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'warehouses': statistics
    }, 200
```

## ๐ฏ ุงููุชุงุฆุฌ ุงููุชููุนุฉ:

โ **ุฃุชูุชุฉ ุงููุฑุงุฑุงุช ุงููุงููุฉ:** ุงููุธุงู ููุฑุฑ ุงูุณุนุฑ ุงูุตุญูุญ ุชููุงุฆูุงู  
โ **ุนูููุงุช ูุญุงุณุจูุฉ ุฏูููุฉ:** ููุงุชูุฑ ููููุฏ ุชููุงุฆูุฉ  
โ **ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ูุฎุฒูู ูุชูุฏูุฉ:** ุชุชุจุน ุดุงูู ููุฃุตูุงู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ูุงููุณุชุนููุฉ ูุงูุชุงููุฉ  
โ **ุฑุคูุฉ ูุงุถุญุฉ:** ูุนุฑูุฉ ุฏูููุฉ ุจุญุงูุฉ ูู ุตูู ููููุนู  
โ **ููุงุกุฉ ุนุงููุฉ:** ุชูููู ุงูุฃุฎุทุงุก ูุงูููุช ุงููุณุชุบุฑู  

---

## ๐ ุงูููุงุญุธุงุช ุงููุงูุฉ:

1. **ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููููุฏ:** ุญุณุงุจ ุชููุงุฆู ุจูุงุกู ุนูู ุงููุชูุณุท
2. **ุณุนุฑ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ:** ูุฎุชูู ุญุณุจ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุงุดุชุฑุงู (ูุดุท/ูููุทุน)
3. **ุฅูุบุงุก ุงูุชุฃููู:** ุชููุงุฆู ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุฑููุฉ ุฅูู STS
4. **ุงููุณุชูุฏุนุงุช ุงูุงูุชุฑุงุถูุฉ:** ุชุชุจุน ุฏููู ููุฃุตูุงู
5. **ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู:** ุงูุฃุตูุงู ุงููุณุชุนููุฉ ุงูุตุงูุญุฉ ูููู ุฅุนุงุฏุฉ ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงููุง

# ุชุตุญูุญ ุญุฑุฌ: ุฑุจุท ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ุจุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
## Critical Correction: Linking Estimated Consumption Invoice to Work Order

**ุงูุฃููููุฉ:** ุนุงููุฉ ุฌุฏุงู  
**ุงูุชุฃุซูุฑ:** ุงููููุฉ 10.4  
**ุงูุญุงูุฉ:** ุชุตุญูุญ ุดุงูู

---

## ๐ฏ ุงููุฏู:

ุถูุงู ุฃู ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ุชููุดุฃ ูุชูุถุงู ุฅูู ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุนููู ูุจู ุฅุชูุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู.

---

## ๐ ุงููุดููุฉ ุงูุณุงุจูุฉ:

โ ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ูุงู ุฎุทูุฉ ูุธุฑูุฉ ููุท  
โ ูู ููู ูุฑุชุจุทุงู ูุจุงุดุฑุฉ ุจุงูููุชุฑุฉ  
โ ูุฏ ูุชู ูุณูุงู ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ  
โ ูุฏ ุชุถูุน ุงููุณุชุญูุงุช ุงููุงููุฉ  

---

## ๐ ุงูุชุตุญูุญ ุงูุดุงูู:

### 10.4.1: ูุญุฏุฉ ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู (ูุญุฏูุซุฉ)

**ุงููุตู:** ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูููููุฏ ูุน ุงูุฑุจุท ุงููุจุงุดุฑ ุจุงูููุชุฑุฉ.

```python
class EstimatedConsumptionCalculator:
    """ุญุงุณุจุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู"""
    
    def __init__(self, subscriber_id, defect_date):
        self.subscriber = Subscriber.query.get(subscriber_id)
        self.defect_date = defect_date
    
    def get_last_valid_reading(self):
        """ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุขุฎุฑ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ุตุญูุญุฉ"""
        
        # ุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุขุฎุฑ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ูุจู ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงูุนุทู
        last_reading = MeterReading.query.filter(
            MeterReading.subscriber_id == self.subscriber.id,
            MeterReading.reading_date < self.defect_date
        ).order_by(MeterReading.reading_date.desc()).first()
        
        if not last_reading:
            return None
        
        return {
            'reading_value': last_reading.reading_value,
            'reading_date': last_reading.reading_date,
            'days_ago': (self.defect_date - last_reading.reading_date).days
        }
    
    def calculate_average_daily_consumption(self):
        """ุญุณุงุจ ูุชูุณุท ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงููููู ูู ุขุฎุฑ 3 ุฃุดูุฑ"""
        
        three_months_ago = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=90)
        
        # ุฌูุจ ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ูู ุขุฎุฑ 3 ุฃุดูุฑ
        recent_invoices = Invoice.query.filter(
            Invoice.subscriber_id == self.subscriber.id,
            Invoice.invoice_type == 'consumption',
            Invoice.issue_date >= three_months_ago
        ).all()
        
        if not recent_invoices:
            return {
                'status': 'error',
                'message': 'ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ููุงุชูุฑ ูุงููุฉ ูุญุณุงุจ ุงููุชูุณุท'
            }
        
        # ุญุณุงุจ ุฅุฌูุงูู ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ูุงูุฃูุงู
        total_consumption = sum([inv.consumption_kwh for inv in recent_invoices])
        total_days = (recent_invoices[-1].issue_date - recent_invoices[0].issue_date).days
        
        if total_days == 0:
            return {
                'status': 'error',
                'message': 'ูุง ูููู ุญุณุงุจ ุงููุชูุณุท'
            }
        
        average_daily = total_consumption / total_days
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'total_consumption': total_consumption,
            'total_days': total_days,
            'average_daily': round(average_daily, 2),
            'invoices_count': len(recent_invoices)
        }
    
    def calculate_estimated_consumption(self):
        """ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ุงููุงูู"""
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 1: ุขุฎุฑ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ุตุญูุญุฉ
        last_reading = self.get_last_valid_reading()
        if not last_reading:
            return {
                'status': 'error',
                'message': 'ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ูุฑุงุกุฉ ุตุญูุญุฉ ุณุงุจูุฉ'
            }
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 2: ูุชูุณุท ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงููููู
        avg_consumption = self.calculate_average_daily_consumption()
        if avg_consumption['status'] != 'success':
            return avg_consumption
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 3: ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู
        days_without_reading = (datetime.now() - last_reading['reading_date']).days
        estimated_consumption = avg_consumption['average_daily'] * days_without_reading
        
        # ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 4: ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุชูููุฉ (ุจุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู ุณุนุฑ ุงูููุฑุจุงุก ุงูุญุงูู)
        electricity_rate = self.get_current_electricity_rate()
        estimated_cost = estimated_consumption * electricity_rate
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'last_reading_date': last_reading['reading_date'].isoformat(),
            'last_reading_value': last_reading['reading_value'],
            'days_without_reading': days_without_reading,
            'average_daily_consumption': avg_consumption['average_daily'],
            'estimated_consumption_kwh': round(estimated_consumption, 2),
            'electricity_rate': electricity_rate,
            'estimated_cost': round(estimated_cost, 2),
            'confidence_level': 'high' if len(avg_consumption['invoices_count']) >= 3 else 'medium'
        }
    
    def get_current_electricity_rate(self):
        """ุงูุญุตูู ุนูู ุณุนุฑ ุงูููุฑุจุงุก ุงูุญุงูู"""
        # ูููู ุฌุนู ูุฐุง ูุชุบูุฑุงู ูู ุงูุฅุนุฏุงุฏุงุช
        return 1.5  # ุฑูุงู ููู ูููููุงุท
```

---

### 10.4.2: ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู (ูุญุฏูุซุฉ)

**ุงููุตู:** ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ ูุฑุจุทูุง ูุจุงุดุฑุฉ ุจุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู.

```python
def create_estimated_consumption_invoice(work_order_id, estimated_consumption_data):
    """
    ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ูุฑุจุทูุง ุจุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
    """
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(work_order_id)
    subscriber = work_order.subscriber
    
    # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุฃู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุตุญูุญุฉ
    if estimated_consumption_data['status'] != 'success':
        return {
            'status': 'error',
            'message': 'ูุง ูููู ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู',
            'details': estimated_consumption_data
        }
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
    invoice = Invoice(
        subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
        invoice_type='estimated_consumption',
        invoice_number=generate_invoice_number(),
        issue_date=datetime.now(),
        due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15),
        status='unpaid',
        total_amount=estimated_consumption_data['estimated_cost'],
        notes=f"ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุณุชููุงู ุชูุฏูุฑู - ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชุงูู ({estimated_consumption_data['days_without_reading']} ููู)"
    )
    
    db.session.add(invoice)
    db.session.flush()  # ููุญุตูู ุนูู invoice_id
    
    # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุจููุฏ ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
    invoice_line = InvoiceLineItem(
        invoice_id=invoice.id,
        item_type='estimated_consumption',
        description=f"ุงุณุชููุงู ุชูุฏูุฑู: {estimated_consumption_data['estimated_consumption_kwh']} ูููููุงุท ร {estimated_consumption_data['electricity_rate']} ุฑูุงู",
        amount=estimated_consumption_data['estimated_cost'],
        quantity=estimated_consumption_data['estimated_consumption_kwh'],
        unit_price=estimated_consumption_data['electricity_rate']
    )
    
    db.session.add(invoice_line)
    
    # ุฑุจุท ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ ุจุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
    work_order.estimated_consumption_invoice_id = invoice.id
    work_order.estimated_consumption_amount = estimated_consumption_data['estimated_cost']
    work_order.estimated_consumption_kwh = estimated_consumption_data['estimated_consumption_kwh']
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจู
    journal_entry = JournalEntry(
        entry_date=datetime.now(),
        description=f"ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุณุชููุงู ุชูุฏูุฑู - {subscriber.name} (ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชุงูู)",
        debit_account='Accounts Receivable',
        debit_amount=estimated_consumption_data['estimated_cost'],
        credit_account='Service Revenue',
        credit_amount=estimated_consumption_data['estimated_cost'],
        reference_id=invoice.id,
        reference_type='invoice'
    )
    
    db.session.add(journal_entry)
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'invoice_id': invoice.id,
        'invoice_number': invoice.invoice_number,
        'amount': estimated_consumption_data['estimated_cost'],
        'consumption_kwh': estimated_consumption_data['estimated_consumption_kwh'],
        'linked_to_work_order': work_order.id
    }

# API ูุญุณุงุจ ูุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู
@app.route('/api/maintenance/defective-meter/create-consumption-invoice', methods=['POST'])
def create_consumption_invoice():
    """
    ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ูุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - work_order_id: ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
    # - subscriber_id: ุงููุดุชุฑู
    # - defect_date: ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงูุนุทู
    
    calculator = EstimatedConsumptionCalculator(
        subscriber_id=data['subscriber_id'],
        defect_date=datetime.fromisoformat(data['defect_date'])
    )
    
    # ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู
    consumption_data = calculator.calculate_estimated_consumption()
    
    if consumption_data['status'] != 'success':
        return consumption_data, 400
    
    # ุนุฑุถ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ููููุธู ููููุงููุฉ
    return {
        'status': 'pending_approval',
        'estimated_consumption_data': consumption_data,
        'message': 'ูุฑุฌู ูุฑุงุฌุนุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ูุงูููุงููุฉ ุนูู ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ'
    }, 200

# API ูุชุฃููุฏ ูุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
@app.route('/api/maintenance/defective-meter/confirm-consumption-invoice', methods=['POST'])
def confirm_consumption_invoice():
    """
    ุชุฃููุฏ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ูุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
    """
    
    data = request.json
    
    # ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุชููุนุฉ:
    # - work_order_id: ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
    # - estimated_consumption_data: ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุงุณุชููุงู
    # - approved_by: ุงูููุธู ุงููุตุฑุญ
    
    result = create_estimated_consumption_invoice(
        work_order_id=data['work_order_id'],
        estimated_consumption_data=data['estimated_consumption_data']
    )
    
    if result['status'] == 'success':
        # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
        work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(data['work_order_id'])
        work_order.consumption_invoice_created = True
        work_order.consumption_invoice_created_date = datetime.now()
        db.session.commit()
    
    return result, 200 if result['status'] == 'success' else 400
```

---

### 10.4.3: ุชุญุฏูุฏ ุชูููุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู (ูุญุฏูุซุฉ)

**ุงููุตู:** ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ูููุตูุฉ ูุชูููุฉ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ.

```python
def create_meter_replacement_invoice(work_order_id, replacement_option):
    """
    ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุชูููุฉ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ
    """
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(work_order_id)
    subscriber = work_order.subscriber
    
    # ุฌูุจ ุณุนุฑ ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ
    meter_item = InventoryItem.query.filter_by(
        item_code='TRADITIONAL-METER'
    ).first()
    
    meter_cost = meter_item.unit_price if meter_item else 2000
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุฏ ุงููุจูุบ ุจูุงุกู ุนูู ุงูุฎูุงุฑ
    if replacement_option == 'full_charge':
        charge_amount = meter_cost
        charge_description = 'ุชุญููู ุงูุชูููุฉ ูุงููุฉ'
    elif replacement_option == 'half_charge':
        charge_amount = meter_cost / 2
        charge_description = 'ุชุญููู 50% ูู ุงูุชูููุฉ'
    elif replacement_option == 'free_replacement':
        charge_amount = 0
        charge_description = 'ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูุฌุงูู (ุถูุงู)'
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ ููุท ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ููุงู ูุจูุบ
    if charge_amount > 0:
        invoice = Invoice(
            subscriber_id=subscriber.id,
            invoice_type='meter_replacement',
            invoice_number=generate_invoice_number(),
            issue_date=datetime.now(),
            due_date=datetime.now() + timedelta(days=15),
            status='unpaid',
            total_amount=charge_amount,
            notes=f"ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุนุฏุงุฏ - {charge_description}"
        )
        
        db.session.add(invoice)
        db.session.flush()
        
        # ุฅุถุงูุฉ ุจูุฏ ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ
        invoice_line = InvoiceLineItem(
            invoice_id=invoice.id,
            item_type='meter_replacement',
            description=f"ุนุฏุงุฏ ุชูููุฏู ุฌุฏูุฏ - {charge_description}",
            amount=charge_amount,
            quantity=1,
            unit_price=meter_cost
        )
        
        db.session.add(invoice_line)
        
        # ุฑุจุท ุงููุงุชูุฑุฉ ุจุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
        work_order.meter_replacement_invoice_id = invoice.id
        work_order.meter_replacement_amount = charge_amount
        
        # ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฏ ูุญุงุณุจู
        journal_entry = JournalEntry(
            entry_date=datetime.now(),
            description=f"ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุนุฏุงุฏ - {subscriber.name}",
            debit_account='Accounts Receivable',
            debit_amount=charge_amount,
            credit_account='Equipment Sales',
            credit_amount=charge_amount,
            reference_id=invoice.id,
            reference_type='invoice'
        )
        
        db.session.add(journal_entry)
        db.session.commit()
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'invoice_id': invoice.id,
            'invoice_number': invoice.invoice_number,
            'amount': charge_amount,
            'linked_to_work_order': work_order.id
        }
    else:
        # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู ุจุฃู ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูุฌุงูู
        work_order.meter_replacement_amount = 0
        work_order.meter_replacement_invoice_id = None
        db.session.commit()
        
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'invoice_id': None,
            'amount': 0,
            'message': 'ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ูุฌุงูู - ูุง ุชูุฌุฏ ูุงุชูุฑุฉ'
        }
```

---

### 10.4.4: ุฅุชูุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู (ูุญุฏูุซุฉ)

**ุงููุตู:** ูุง ูููู ุฅุบูุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู ุฅูุง ุจุนุฏ ุฅูุดุงุก ุฌููุน ุงูููุงุชูุฑ.

```python
def complete_defective_meter_replacement(work_order_id, new_meter_serial, seal_serial, breaker_serial):
    """
    ุฅุชูุงู ุนูููุฉ ุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุงูุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุชุงูู
    ูุฌุจ ุฃู ุชููู ุฌููุน ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ูุฏ ุฃููุดุฆุช ูุจู ูุฐู ุงูุฎุทูุฉ
    """
    
    work_order = MaintenanceWorkOrder.query.get(work_order_id)
    
    # ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุฃู ุฌููุน ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ูุฏ ุฃููุดุฆุช
    if not work_order.consumption_invoice_created:
        return {
            'status': 'error',
            'message': 'ูุฌุจ ุฅูุดุงุก ูุงุชูุฑุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู ุฃููุงู'
        }, 400
    
    if work_order.meter_replacement_amount is None:
        return {
            'status': 'error',
            'message': 'ูุฌุจ ุชุญุฏูุฏ ุชูููุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุฃููุงู'
        }, 400
    
    # ุงูุจุญุซ ุนู ุงูููููุงุช ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
    new_meter = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=new_meter_serial,
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    new_seal = InventoryUnit.query.filter_by(
        serial_number=seal_serial,
        status='issued'
    ).first()
    
    if not new_meter or not new_seal:
        return {
            'status': 'error',
            'message': 'ุฃุญุฏ ุงูููููุงุช ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ุบูุฑ ููุฌูุฏ'
        }, 400
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูููููุงุช ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ
    new_meter.status = 'installed'
    new_meter.installed_at_subscriber_id = work_order.subscriber_id
    new_meter.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    new_seal.status = 'installed'
    new_seal.installed_at_subscriber_id = work_order.subscriber_id
    new_seal.installation_date = datetime.now()
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ููู ุงููุดุชุฑู
    subscriber = work_order.subscriber
    subscriber.meter_serial = new_meter_serial
    subscriber.seal_serial = seal_serial
    
    # ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
    work_order.status = 'completed'
    work_order.completion_date = datetime.now()
    work_order.completed_by = current_user.username
    
    # ุฅูุดุงุก ููุฎุต ูุงูู ูุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
    work_order.total_invoices_amount = (
        work_order.estimated_consumption_amount + 
        work_order.meter_replacement_amount
    )
    
    db.session.commit()
    
    return {
        'status': 'success',
        'work_order_id': work_order.id,
        'completion_date': work_order.completion_date.isoformat(),
        'financial_summary': {
            'estimated_consumption_invoice': work_order.estimated_consumption_amount,
            'meter_replacement_invoice': work_order.meter_replacement_amount,
            'total_amount': work_order.total_invoices_amount
        },
        'message': 'ุชู ุฅุชูุงู ุนูููุฉ ุงูุงุณุชุจุฏุงู ุจูุฌุงุญ. ุชู ุฅูุดุงุก ุฌููุน ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ูุฅุถุงูุชูุง ุฅูู ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุนููู.'
    }, 200

# API ูุฅุชูุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู
@app.route('/api/maintenance/defective-meter/complete', methods=['POST'])
def complete_replacement_work_order():
    """ุฅุชูุงู ุฃูุฑ ุงูุนูู ุจุนุฏ ุงูุชุญูู ูู ุฌููุน ุงูููุงุชูุฑ"""
    
    data = request.json
    
    result = complete_defective_meter_replacement(
        work_order_id=data['work_order_id'],
        new_meter_serial=data['new_meter_serial'],
        seal_serial=data['seal_serial'],
        breaker_serial=data['breaker_serial']
    )
    
    return result
```

---

## ๐ ุณูุฑ ุงูุนูู ุงููุงูู (Updated Workflow):

```

โ  - ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู = ูุชูุณุท ร ุฃูุงู ุงูุนุทู               โ

                         โ
โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
โ  ุงูุฎุทูุฉ 2: ุนุฑุถ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ููููุธู + ุงูููุงููุฉ                  โ
โ  โ ุงูููุงููุฉ ุนูู ุงูุงุณุชููุงู ุงูุชูุฏูุฑู                        โ
```

#### 3.3 (ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ): ุชุญุฏูุซ "ุชุทุจูู ุงูููู ุงูููุฏุงูู" ูุฏุนู ุญุฒู ุงูุนูู

**ุงููุฏู:** ุชูููู ูุงุฏุฉ ุงููุฑู ูู ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงูุญุฒู ูุงูููุงู

**ุงูููุงู:**
- ุนุฑุถ "ุญุฒูุฉ ุงูุนูู" ุงููุณูุฏุฉ ุจุฏูุงู ูู ุงูููุงู ุงููุฑุฏูุฉ
- ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงูููุงู ุงููุฑุนูุฉ ุฏุงุฎู ุงูุญุฒูุฉ
- ุชุญุฏูุซ ุญุงูุฉ ูู ูููุฉ ูุฑุนูุฉ ุนูู ุญุฏุฉ
- ุฒุฑ "ุฅููุงู ุงูุญุฒูุฉ" ุนูุฏ ุฅูุฌุงุฒ ุฌููุน ุงูููุงู

**ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุชุทุจูู:**

#### 3.4 (ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ): ุชุทููุฑ "ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงููุงุญุต/ูุฑุงูุจ ุงูุฌูุฏุฉ"

### ุงูููุงู ุงููุฑุนูุฉ ุงูููุตุญุญุฉ:

#### 3.1 (ุฌุฏูุฏ): ุชุทููุฑ ูุญุฏุฉ "ุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงูุฎุทุท ูุงููุดุงุฑูุน"

**ุงููุฏู:** ููุทุฉ ุงูุจุฏุงูุฉ ุนูู ุงููุณุชูู ุงูุฅุฏุงุฑู ุงูุฃุนูู

**ุงูููุงู:**
- ุดุงุดุฉ ููุฅุฏุงุฑุฉ ุงูุนููุง ูุฅูุดุงุก "ุฎุทุฉ ุนูู" ุฃู "ูุดุฑูุน" ุฌุฏูุฏ
- ุชุญุฏูุฏ:
  * ุงุณู ุงููุดุฑูุน (ูุซุงู: "ูุดุฑูุน ุชุฑุญูู ุญู ุงูุณูุงู ุฅูู IoT - ุงููุฑุญูุฉ ุงูุฃููู")
  * ุงูุฃูุฏุงู ุงูุนุงูุฉ
  * ุงูููุฒุงููุฉ ุงูุชูุฏูุฑูุฉ
  * ุงููุญุทุฉ ุงููุณุคููุฉ ุนู ุงูุชูููุฐ (ูุซูุงู: ูุญุทุฉ ุงูุญุฏูุฏุฉ)
  * ุงูุฌุฏูู ุงูุฒููู ุงููุชููุน

- ุฏูุฑุฉ ุญูุงุฉ ุงูุฎุทุฉ:
  * **ููุชุฑุญุฉ (Proposed):** ุชู ุงูุฅูุดุงุกุ ุงูุชุธุงุฑ ุงูููุงููุฉ
  * **ูุนุชูุฏุฉ (Approved):** ุฌุงูุฒุฉ ููุชุฌุฒุฆุฉ ูุงูุชูููุฐ
  * **ููุฏ ุงูุชูููุฐ (In Progress):** ุญุฒู ุงูุนูู ููุฏ ุงูุฅูุฌุงุฒ
  * **ููุชููุฉ (Completed):** ุฌููุน ุงูุญุฒู ููุงูู ุนูููุง

**ูุซุงู ุนูู ูุดุฑูุน:**

#### 19.2: ุชุตููู "ููุญุฉ ุงูุชุญูู ุงูุฌุบุฑุงููุฉ ุงูููุญุฏุฉ" (Unified GIS Dashboard)

**ุงููุฏู:** ูุงุฌูุฉ ุฑุฆูุณูุฉ ุชูุถุญ ุงูุดุจูุฉ ุจุงููุงูู ูุน ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุญูุฉ

#### 20.3: ุชุทุจูู "ููุชุฑุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช" ุนูู ูุณุชูู ุงููุธุงู

**ุงููุฏู:** ุชุนุฏูู ูู ุงุณุชุนูุงู ูู ุงููุธุงู ููุดูู ุดุฑุท "ุงูููุงู ุงูุชูุธููู"

**ุงููุจุฏุฃ ุงูุฃุณุงุณู:**

```

1. ูููุฉ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ุงูุญุงูู

3. ุงูููุงูุงุช ุงูุชูุธูููุฉ ุงูุชู ููููู ุงููุตูู ุฅูููุง

```

**ุฃูุซูุฉ ุนูู ุงูุงุณุชุนูุงูุงุช:**

```
ูุซุงู 1: ูุฏูุฑ ูุญุทุฉ G1 ููุชุญ ููุญุฉ ุงูุชุญูู
โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

โ SELECT * FROM live_data                            โ
โ                                                     โ

โ WHERE station_id = 'G1'                            โ
โ AND user_role = 'station_manager'                  โ
โ AND user_id = 'ahmed'                              โ
โ                                                     โ

โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
```

**ุชุทุจูู ุงูููุชุฑุฉ ุนูู ุฌููุน ุงููุญุฏุงุช:**

#### 24.2: ุชุญุฏูุซ "ุชุทุจูู ุงูููู/ุงููุดุบู" ูุฏุนู ุฌููุงุช ุงููุฑุงุกุฉ

### ุงูุชูุงูู ูุน ุจููุฉ ุงูุฃูุธูุฉ

#### 29.3: ุฃุชูุชุฉ "ุนูููุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูู ุงูุนูุณู"

#### 30.2: ูุญุฏุฉ "ุงูููุงุชูุฑ ูุงูุฏูุน ุงูุฅููุชุฑููู"

#### 30.3: ูุญุฏุฉ "ูุฑุงูุจุฉ ุงูุงุณุชููุงู" (ููุดุชุฑูู IoT)

**ุงููุฏู:** ุฅุนุทุงุก ุงูุนููู ุฑุคูุฉ ุญูุฉ ูุงุณุชููุงูู

- ุฑุคูุฉ ุญูุฉ ููุงุณุชููุงู

#### 30.4: ูุญุฏุฉ "ุงูุฏุนู ุงูููู ูุทูุจุงุช ุงูุฎุฏูุฉ"

**ุงููุฏู:** ุฑูููุฉ ุนูููุฉ ุทูุจ ุงูุฏุนู ุงูููู

- ุฅูุดุงุก ุทูุจ ุณูู
- ุชุชุจุน ุญู ููุทูุจ

#### 30.5: ูุญุฏุฉ "ูุฑูุฒ ุงููุณุงุนุฏุฉ ูุฎุฏูุฉ ุงูุนููุงุก"

**ุงููุฏู:** ุชูููุฑ ููุงุฉ ุชูุงุตู ูุนุงูุฉ

#### 30.6: ูุธุงู ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช (Push Notifications)

**ุงููุฏู:** ุงูุชูุงุตู ุงูุงุณุชุจุงูู ูุน ุงูุนููู

**ุฃููุงุน ุงูุฅุดุนุงุฑุงุช:**

```

โโ "ูุงุชูุฑุชู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ุฌุงูุฒุฉ! ุงููุจูุบ: 450 ุฑูุงู"
```

#### 32.1: ุจูุงุก ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูููุฑุฏูู

**ุงููุงูุน ุงูุญุงูู:**
- ูุงุฆูุฉ ุงูููุฑุฏูู ูุชูุงุซุฑุฉ ูู ุงูููุงุชู ูุงูุฏูุงุชุฑ
- ูุนูููุงุช ุบูุฑ ููุญุฏุฉ ูุบูุฑ ูุญุฏุซุฉ
- ุตุนูุจุฉ ูู ุงููุตูู ุงูุณุฑูุน ููุจูุงูุงุช

#### 32.3: ุชุทููุฑ ุนูููุฉ ุฃูุฑ ุงูุดุฑุงุก (Purchase Order - PO)

```
    โ
```

### ุงููููุฉ 33: ุจูุงุก ูุญุฏุฉ ุงููุญุงุณุจุฉ ุงููุงููุฉ ุงููุชูุงููุฉ
